Niu Lan Couple Returned to Detention Center 90

Currently Detained in the Detention Center's VIP Room

Trial Scheduled for the 10th of this Month

Due to their hunger strike last month, Niu Lan and his wife were bailed out by Soong Ching-ling, Cai Yuanpei, Yang Xingfo, and others to the Jiangsu High Court and sent to Gulou Hospital for treatment. They have now fully recovered. The Jiangsu High Court has scheduled the trial for the 10th of this month. Niu Lan and his wife also submitted a request to the Jiangsu High Court yesterday to be returned to the detention center to await trial. The court then dispatched the warden of the detention center, Xi Kuan, along with police officers, to Gulou Hospital at 5 p.m. on the 5th to return Niu Lan and his wife to the detention center. The details are as follows: ▲ Decision to Return After Niu Lan and his wife were sent to Gulou Hospital for treatment, they recovered quickly. Gulou Hospital sent four letters to the Jiangsu High Court requesting that Niu Lan and his wife be returned. The court initially intended to return them earlier, but because the trial was scheduled for the 10th of this month, to avoid any unforeseen circumstances, they planned to return them the day before the trial. However, Niu Lan and his wife believed that they had fully recovered and that the court had specially prepared a VIP room for them, so they also wished to return to the detention center as soon as possible to await trial. They submitted a request to the Jiangsu High Court on the 4th, requesting immediate return. The Jiangsu High Court, seeing that Niu Lan and his wife wished to return early, decided to go to pick them up on the 5th.

▲Pre-Arrangements After the Jiangsu High Court decided to pick them up on the 5th, they dispatched personnel to Gulou Hospital at 2 p.m. that afternoon to settle the accounts. It was calculated that Niu Lan and his wife had been hospitalized for a total of 19 days from the 17th of last month to the present day, with all expenses totaling over 400 yuan, which were paid in full by the Jiangsu High Court. For the sake of strict security, the Jiangsu High Court also sent a letter to the Capital Police Department requesting them to send police officers to escort them. The department dispatched the captain of the special task force, Li Fanqing, leading 40 armed police officers, to Gulou Hospital before 2 p.m. to pick them up. The four military police officers and four court police officers originally stationed at the hospital also assisted in the security. Two large cars were prepared for transportation. At that time, the crowd outside Gulou Hospital reached as many as one or two hundred people, all wanting to see the faces of Niu Lan and his wife.

▲Letter Delivered to the Hospital The Jiangsu High Court also sent a letter to Gulou Hospital in advance, notifying them of the return of Niu Lan and his wife. The letter stated, "[Regarding the case of Niu Lan and others endangering the Republic of China, which this court has accepted, previously, Niu Lan and others became ill due to a hunger strike and should be treated. A warrant was issued, and the Jiangning District Court Prosecutor was requested to dispatch military police to bring Niu Lan, Wang Deli, and Zeng, two individuals, to your hospital for treatment. Now, there is a need to bring Niu Lan and others back for questioning. In addition to sending a letter to the Jiangning District Court Prosecutor to dispatch military police to pick them up, we hereby request your hospital to hand over Niu Lan, Wang Deli, and Zeng, two individuals, to the Jiangning District Court Prosecutor for questioning. Respectfully addressed to the Director of Nanjing Gulou Hospital, Lin Biao, President of Jiangsu High Court, signed by Li Mian, Acting Presiding Judge of Jiangsu High Court]."

▲Escorted Back to the Court At 4:45 p.m., Xi Kuan, the warden of the Jiangning District Court Detention Center responsible for the pick-up, arrived at Gulou Hospital and went to the ward where Niu Lan and his wife were staying, informing them of the intention to return. Niu Lan and his wife both expressed their willingness. The court police then carried Niu Lan and his wife's luggage, totaling eight pieces, onto the large car. Niu Lan and his wife walked out of the hospital side by side. Niu Lan expressed his gratitude to the staff of Gulou Hospital, saying, "Take care, see you again." Niu Lan was still wearing a Western-style suit with a lapel shirt and yellow leather shoes, while his wife was wearing a white silk Western-style suit and black satin Chinese-style slippers. Both of them had regained their original spirits and physical condition. After Niu Lan and his wife boarded the large car, they sat face to face in the front. Twelve police officers and four court police officers sat on both sides in order. Another large car was filled with police officers, and four military police officers sat in a small car. Xi Kuan and court officials also sat in another small car. At around 5 p.m., the large car carrying Niu Lan and his wife started first, followed by the military police car, Xi Kuan's car, and two motorcycles from the police department, and then another large car. They went straight to the Jiangning District Court along Zhongshan Road, arriving at 6 p.m.

▲Sent to the Detention Center After Niu Lan and his wife arrived at the Jiangning District Court, they were escorted to the detention center by county police. The detention center had specially prepared two VIP rooms for Niu Lan and his wife. The rooms were originally the detention center's treatment rooms, which were quite spacious and had screens installed, expressing satisfaction.

▲Trial Scheduled The Jiangsu High Court has scheduled the trial for the 10th of this month. Subpoenas have been delivered to Niu Lan and his wife, and subpoenas for witnesses have also been sent to the Jiangsu High Court Second Branch in Shanghai for substituted service. All are expected to arrive in Nanjing on time for the court hearing.

Legislative Yuan Reviews Ministry of Education Organization Act 91

Deemed No Revision Necessary

At the 196th meeting of the Legislative Yuan on the 6th, the Legal System Committee of the Yuan reported on its review of the revised draft of the Ministry of Education Organization Act. The gist of the review: (1) No revision is necessary for the Ministry of Education Organization Act; (2) The establishment of the National Compilation and Translation Bureau without legislative procedure should be questioned. It was resolved that the review report be adopted. The original report is recorded as follows: [This case was resolved by the 191st meeting of this Yuan and referred to this committee for review. In compliance, discussions were held at the 159th, 160th, and 161st meetings of this committee. It was generally agreed that reviewing educational books, instruments, and other educational supplies is an important function of educational administration and should be handled by the Ministry of Education itself. The revised draft transfers the review of educational books, specimens, instruments, and other educational supplies for schools below the secondary level to the National Compilation and Translation Bureau, with only the review and approval matters listed in the responsibilities of the General Education Department. The authority is inconsistent, and the handling is likely to be obstructed. The current regulations of the Ministry of Education Organization Act are more appropriate and do not require revision. As for the attached draft of the National Compilation and Translation Bureau Organization Regulations, as stipulated in Article 4 of the regulations, it is essentially a disguised expansion of the Editing and Compilation Department of the Ministry of Education, which is not commensurate with the name. Moreover, it concerns the organization of national agencies, and its promulgation and implementation by ministerial order without legislative procedure is a clear violation of legislative authority and should be questioned by this Yuan in accordance with the law. Whether all the review results are appropriate is reported accordingly and respectfully submitted to the general assembly for public resolution.]

Kunshan 93

Autopsy Ordered in Case of Woman Beaten to Death by Family Members Gu, the daughter-in-law of Wu Haibo of Xiximen Waima Guanxiatang, was usually abused by her parents-in-law and repeatedly blamed for no reason. On the 29th of last month, Gu was severely beaten by her family members again and took the opportunity to escape. However, she was found and brought back by her mother-in-law and suffered even more beatings. She died from her injuries at 4 p.m. Wu immediately purchased a coffin and prepared for burial. The incident was discovered by Zhu Junxian, the deputy chief of the town, who requested Han Shouyi, the patrol captain of the local police station, to investigate. However, the Wu family bribed the patrol captain, Han, who disregarded everything and reported to the precinct officer Yuan Yingqiu that she had died by suicide. Officer Gu did not examine the facts and was deceived by Han. Neighbors, dissatisfied with the report, requested the general bureau to send personnel to investigate. The bureau chief immediately dispatched Inspector Zhang Tian to investigate and learned that Gu had indeed died from beatings. Wu Haibo, his wife Sun, his son Jinsheng, and his daughters Qu and Jia were taken to the bureau to be interrogated and then escorted to the county for questioning. They all claimed that Gu had died by suicide. The two daughters were released on bail in court. However, the news of Gu's death being due to beating spread throughout the city. The next day, five neighbors and eighteen merchants from Xiximen jointly petitioned the county government to order an autopsy and provided a guarantee. After receiving the petition, the county government stated that the matter was significant and difficult to approve without a petition from the deceased's relatives. On the 3rd, Gu's mother, Chen, and maternal uncle, Chen Naifen, learned of the incident in Shanghai and came to Kunshan to petition the county government to order an autopsy to clarify the cause of death. Chen Ying, the trial officer, accompanied by the autopsy official and the Wu family, including Wu Haibo, went to open the coffin for examination. The examination revealed that the deceased had bruises all over her body, with dozens of injuries. However, Trial Officer Chen only instructed Wu Haibo to re-coffin Gu and ordered the headman to guard the coffin. He also told Gu's mother, Chen, and Chen Naifen, that the injuries of the deceased had been examined and would be investigated further. Observers at the scene, believing that Trial Officer Chen and the autopsy official were handling the corpse perfunctorily, immediately protested, almost surrounding Chen. Later, patrol officers protected Chen and others, allowing them to return safely.

Rental Disputes After Military Conflict Since the January 28th Shanghai Incident, all businesses in this county have been greatly affected. After the Japanese army invaded the territory on March 1st, they all suspended operations one after another until the signing of the peace treaty, when they gradually resumed business. The direct and indirect losses were enormous. After the resumption of business, the businesses that rented premises organized a Tenants' Association to request landlords to waive rent for several months as a gesture of sympathy. Meetings were held repeatedly, but few landlords attended. In desperation, they jointly petitioned the authorities, requesting them to uphold justice, but to no avail. As a result, the disputes remain unresolved and conflicts arise from time to time. The other day, the Yilimei Foreign Goods Store and others requested the landlord Hu Qiwei to waive two months' rent, but Hu refused, insisting that the store had not suffered direct losses. Conflicts arose between the two sides, and neither would give way. Fortunately, Mr. Zhou Fuchang came forward to mediate and resolved the matter by waiving one month's rent.

Wuxi 95

▲Record of a Defamation Case The resident Bao Yi, because lawyer Zhang Tongjin was hired as the legal counsel of the Lao Zhenghe Dyeing Factory by Chen Eryu in August of last year, suddenly represented another client, Wang Yunzhong, in May of this year, filing a lawsuit against Chen Eryu to demand the surrender of premises, believing that the lawyer had violated the Lawyers' Regulations. He immediately sent a letter to the Suzhou-Wuxi Lawyers' Association, requesting that the matter be referred to the superior supervisory authority for full punishment. At the same time, he sent the draft letter to the local newspaper for publication. He also filed a complaint with the County Court Prosecutor's Office, accusing the lawyer of violating regulations. After seeing the report in the newspaper, Zhang Tongjin believed that Bao Yi was spreading words and defaming his reputation. He immediately filed a private prosecution with the court and sent a letter to various newspapers for correction. The letter stated, "[Who is Bao Yi? Is the community still aware that he is the one who accused people of consuming opium, infringing upon this lawyer's lawful execution of duties?]" After reading the newspaper, Bao Yi also believed that Zhang Tongjin was defaming his reputation. He immediately filed a counterclaim with the court and published a warning to Zhang Tongjin in the newspaper. After seeing the warning, Zhang Tongjin immediately published a solemn announcement, stating, "[This lawyer has always respected morality, justice, law-abidingness, and loyalty in the lawful execution of duties, hence attracting the jealousy of petty people who conspire to undermine this lawyer's credibility.]" After reading the newspaper, Bao Yi immediately published an advertisement in the newspaper, seeking information about Zhang Tongjin's deeds of respecting morality, justice, and law-abidingness. Zhang Tongjin believed that Bao Yi was publicly insulting him and filed another charge of insult with the court. Bao Yi further filed a charge of false accusation against Zhang with the court. It was a mixed bag, demonstrating the ultimate legal struggle. At 12 p.m. on the 5th (the day before yesterday), Judge Wang Kequan opened the court for this case. Bao Yi hired lawyer Sun Zuhong to appear in court to defend him. Both sides engaged in a heated debate, speaking eloquently for a long time. Finally, Zhang Tongjin requested to withdraw the private prosecution in court. Bao Yi's lawyer immediately stood up and stated that he would not withdraw the counterclaim. As a result, Judge Wang instructed them to await further summons for verification and handling, and then adjourned the court.

The merchants should strive to do so.

National Defense Fee Collection Method The Provincial Committee for the Prohibition of Enemy Goods held its sixth meeting yesterday and resolved: (1) The deadline for the National Defense Fee reporting period will be from September onwards, with the 1st, 11th, and 21st of each month being the payment dates. Those before September 1st must be paid by the end of August; (2) Stores that fail to pay the National Defense Fee for more than one ten-day period will be suspended from the public sale of enemy goods, except for those without enemy goods transactions; (3) The National Defense Fee Management Committee is informed that the use of the National Defense Fee must be approved by this meeting and notified by letter.

Changshu 102

▲Dragon Boat Race Outside the South Gate Causes Disaster Since the beginning of summer this year, the weather has been hot, and epidemics have been rampant, with many who contract the disease dying. According to the investigation and statistics of the Public Security Bureau, as of the end of July, no fewer than 500 people have died from epidemics. In the Xitang Qiao area of the fifth district, coffins are nowhere to be bought. The severity of the epidemic can be seen in general. Then, well-wishers, in order to drive away plagues and exorcise evil spirits, launched a dragon lantern procession. Every night, gongs and drums could be heard everywhere. The Public Security Bureau, fearing that it would cause trouble, issued a notice prohibiting it and ordered Yang Jinhai, the leader, to write a guarantee. The matter was then suspended. However, as soon as the dragon lantern procession ended, a dragon king procession was launched. As a result, dragon kings could be seen every ten steps and every five steps along the streets, with colored lanterns hanging high and sincere prayers offered, hoping for abundant rainfall. The other day, Yang Jinhai still took the lead in promoting dragon boat races. At about 10 p.m. on the 5th, while the dragon boat race was in progress, a passenger boat carrying many passengers went to watch. The passengers stood high on the boat, causing it to capsize. All the passengers were submerged. After people tried their best to rescue them for about half an hour, many people were rescued. However, Gu Shanren, Wang Xiangbao, and Zhu Xiaojin, all three locals, had already died. Yang Jinhai, the leader of the event, upon hearing the news, believed that he was responsible for the incident and fainted. The Public Security Bureau, upon hearing the news, immediately dispatched personnel to investigate and confirmed the facts. On the one hand, they immediately arrested Yang Jinhai, the leader. On the other hand, they removed the precinct officer of the area, Fang Desheng, from his post for failing to prevent the incident beforehand and for failing to resolve the disaster afterwards.

Wang Jingwei Came to Shanghai Yesterday Morning and Suddenly Submitted His Resignation to the Central Government 103

Telegraphs Zhang Xueliang Requesting Resignation to Apologize to the Nation

Huang Shaoxiong to Concurrently Act as Representative of the Executive Yuan

Wang's Resignation Intention Is Firm, His Whereabouts in Shanghai Are Secret

Wang Jingwei, the President of the Executive Yuan, recently felt that foreign affairs and financial issues were thorny, and his attitude suddenly turned negative. At 6:20 yesterday morning, Wang, accompanied by Zeng Zhongming, the Vice Minister of Railways, and Tang Youren, his secretary, arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing by special train. He once visited Song Ziwen, the Minister of Finance, to explain the pain of having to resign and asked Song to go to Nanjing immediately to act as the President of the Executive Yuan. At noon, he sent five resignation telegrams to the Central Executive Committee, Chairman Lin of the National Government, Military Commission Chairman Jiang, the ministers of various departments, and Zhang Xueliang. Wang did not return to his residence all day yesterday, and his whereabouts were very secret. He was originally scheduled to receive reporters from various newspapers at 4:00 pm yesterday, but his secretary temporarily brought a handwritten note from Wang to the reporters, saying that he could not meet with them due to business. There were five telegrams to be published. It can be seen that Wang's intention to resign is very firm. Details and the text of the resignation telegram are recorded below.

▲ Visiting Song Ziwen Wang's special train consisted of two carriages, which left Nanjing at 9:30 the night before last and arrived at Zhenru Station at 6:20 yesterday morning. Chen Xinghan, the director of the two railway bureaus, personally waited at the station and arranged everything with strict precautions, refusing reporters to enter the platform. Wang was wearing a white silk gown yesterday, hurriedly left the station and boarded a car, looking quite unhappy. After returning to his residence and taking a short rest, he visited Song Ziwen, the Minister of Finance, stating that he had already resigned and begged Song to return to Nanjing immediately as the Vice President of the Executive Yuan to act as the President of the Executive Yuan. After talking until about 9:00, Wang left. He then met with Chen Gongbo, Zeng Zhongming, and others to discuss everything. At about 11:00, Wang went to Dr. Nauer's hospital on Avenue Joffre to have Dr. Nauer examine his illness. He rested at a friend's place in the afternoon, and his whereabouts were extremely secret.

▲ Main Reason for Wang's Resignation The outside world has speculated a lot about Wang's sudden resignation. Wang himself has made it very clear in his telegram to Zhang Xueliang. Therefore, the financial problem is the main reason for Wang's resignation. When Song Ziwen, the Minister of Finance, resigned and came to Shanghai last time, Wang came to Shanghai repeatedly to persuade him to stay, and even said that he would leave together. After Song resumed his post, he was planning to plan the central government's financial measures, but Rehe suddenly became urgent again. Wang repeatedly telegraphed Zhang to send troops, but he used the excuse of lack of funds and equipment and never gave a satisfactory reply. At the same time, military expenses for suppressing bandits and other items required money everywhere. Wang felt the pain of having no rice to cook, and the saying that the Lushan Conference would be held again could not be realized for a while. Therefore, Wang had to take the resolute path of resignation.

At about 9:00 pm the night before last, a bomb exploded at Maochang Foreign Goods Store, No. 347, Minquan Road. Yun Huifang, a 16-year-old youth, was arrested by the police on duty. After Director Xu of the First Section of the Second District questioned him and found a letter on his person, he sent him to the General Bureau overnight because the circumstances were serious. At about 10:00 yesterday morning, Xie Zao, a staff member of the Third Section, designated by Wu Zhiquan, the head of the Third Section, interrogated him. Yun confessed without denial and made anti-Japanese remarks because of his hot-blooded impulse. Xie stopped him because it was not within the scope of the case. It is now learned that Yun Huifang is under the legal age and because of the anti-Japanese movement, many parties are willing to guarantee him and ask for leniency. However, the Bureau is in the process of investigating and has not made any statement.

Yun Huifang, a patriotic teenager from the Blood Soul Eradication Group, threw a bomb at Maochang Foreign Goods Store, No. 347, Minquan Road, in the French Concession the night before last. After being arrested by the police of the First Branch of the Second District of the Public Security Bureau, Director Xu considered the case to be serious and sent him to the General Bureau at 11:00 that night. Director Wen immediately agreed and sent Yun to the detective to the Police Station. After the head of the Police Station interrogated Yun in detail, he recognized that Yun was completely an underage child, expressed forgiveness, and advised Yun in person. It is expected that Yun will still have to be sent back to the Public Security Bureau in one or two days.

▲ Comply with the Resolutions of the Members' Meeting

▲ Implement the Economic Severance with Japan

▲ Do Not Dye Cut-off Machine Heads and Piece Heads

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday, based on the resolutions of the members' meeting many times, sent letters to various industries, earnestly admonishing them to implement the economic severance with Japan and quickly stop privately importing Japanese goods, and also sent letters to various dyeing industry groups, telling them not to dye cut-off machine heads and piece heads to prevent confusion. The original letter is recorded as follows.

▲ Notice to Various Industries Dear Sirs, Since the Japanese occupied Shenyang on September 18 last year, this Association convened a temporary general meeting of member representatives on September 28 to discuss methods for dealing with national difficulties. Among the important resolutions, there are the following items: (3) Thorough and permanent economic severance with Japan. If any buying and selling with Japan is found, the people will strictly judge the case; (4) Notify the silver and money houses to stop providing loans to merchants dealing in Japanese goods from now on. If any violations are found, they will be regarded as undermining the anti-Japanese movement; (5) Notify various industry associations to establish Japanese goods inspection teams from now on to conduct self-inspection. All of this is to show the determination of merchants to automatically resist goods and increase the country's long-term strength to resist insults. From a general point of view, if this resolution can be followed consistently, then Japanese goods imported into Shanghai should have disappeared long ago. However, from November last year to March this year, Japanese goods imported from Central China, although reduced to 80% to 84%, gradually returned to normal afterwards, becoming more and more prosperous. As for the recent reports, there have been cases of one shipment arriving with more than 16,000 pieces, and the total value of the bills issued is as high as 20 million yuan, which is shocking. To this end, people are approaching step by step, gaining three provinces and gradually plotting North China, while we regard it as a past event and forget it indifferently. With such a bloodless and spineless nation, how can we be worthy of the world? Therefore, the loss of land is not painful, but only the shamelessness of serving the enemy and being slaughtered by others is painful. Merchants have suffered from economic aggression and the scars of the Shanghai War in recent years, and they should have realized this early and stood on the people's front line as the vanguard of resisting insults. However, they have turned to be driven by their own private interests, willing to be spurned and scolded by all parties without repentance. What about the personality of the business community? Therefore, this Association dares to warn the compatriots in the entire business community that if the trafficking of Japanese goods continues, it is no different from jointly destroying our China. The only difference is that the Japanese contribute their efforts, and our merchants contribute their funds. This Association clearly knows that there are many self-respecting people in the business community. However, recently, the import of Japanese goods has been so prosperous. If there is no way out, how can there be a source? The situation in this regard cannot be denied by empty words. Reports from all parties are coming one after another, and they cannot be said to be unfounded. I hope that all merchants in our city will correct their mistakes if they have them and encourage themselves if they don't. Each industry association should have the ambition to never allow any slackness and restrain its members so that they will no longer leave themselves open to criticism. Merchants who are used to trafficking in Japanese goods should not say that they have been in business for a long time and cannot change their business. You must know that you can choose domestic or Western goods as you please. If you have sufficient capital, how difficult is it to find another way out? If the government had decided to resist after the Shenyang Incident, and the Japanese goods merchants had been in a state of war and blockade until now, would they rather give up and wait for death and seek to change their business? This shows that they must not be so. The Japanese goods merchants have always thought that selling Japanese goods is the best option, and they are also mistaken by this idea of ​​苟安. At this time when the national crisis is becoming more and more pressing, if you want to sell Japanese goods for a long time, you will definitely not be allowed by the environment. Instead of ending up in disgrace and ruin, why not change your plans as soon as possible? I hope you will consider the words of medicine and stone calmly.

▲ Advice to Merchants Our country's economic severance with Japan was originally intended to resist Japan's aggression against the Northeast. Now, Japan has publicly declared to the world about the Northeast that it has occupied that it will never return it to China, and even further has the act of forcing Rehe and attacking Tianjin and Beiping. Our country should intensify its resistance to make Japanese goods never have the chance to revive in China, or it may promote their awareness. However, you suddenly import a large amount of Japanese goods at this time, so that Japanese businessmen will restore their original state and carry out activities on a large scale, increasing their economic strength to prepare for the conquest of the entire China. The Japanese want to use those who destroy the Northeast to destroy China, and the traitorous merchants who sell Japanese goods are helping them from the side. To put it simply, it is no different from jointly destroying our China, with the Japanese contributing their efforts and the traitorous merchants contributing their money. I am extremely heartbroken, and I am especially writing to advise you, hoping that you will quickly stop the act of privately importing Japanese goods, otherwise it will be difficult to escape the sanctions of society.

Japanese Warships Protect Cargo Transportation 107

▲ Four Measures Formulated to Be Implemented Starting from the 4th

▲ Japanese Merchants Request Strict Prohibition of Anti-Japanese Groups

Armed Protection of Japanese Goods Transportation to the Yangtze River Estuary Dumping Measures

Organizations and Zuojinsi, Commander of the Third Fleet of the Japanese Navy, have completed discussions. However, Zuojinsi handed over the matter entirely to Sugisaka, Commander of the Marine Corps, because he was about to go on巡武漢 in a few days. Starting from the resumption of Japanese shipping on August 1, armed protection of Japanese goods will be carried out to dump them in the Yangtze River Estuary. The reporter of Shiwenshe specially inquired about various news from the Japanese side yesterday and recorded them as follows.

▲ Armed Protection of Cargo Transportation After Commander Zuojinsi of the First Fleet transferred full authority to Commander Sugisaka of the Marine Corps to handle the armed protection of cargo transportation, Commander Sugisaka immediately issued a letter to overseas Chinese the day before yesterday, detailing his determination to provide armed protection for cargo transportation. At the same time, he summoned important figures from various businesses in Shanghai to discuss the implementation measures. It was immediately formulated that (1) starting from the 4th of this month, for Japanese goods transported from Shanghai to the Yangtze River Estuary area, before the cargo ships have set sail, four warships will be transferred from the First Foreign Fleet to Wuhu, Jiujiang, Hankou, Yichang, and other destinations where Japanese goods are unloaded, to wait for the cargo ships to arrive and implement armed protection for unloading; (2) On the cargo ships departing from Shanghai, officers D. Yuhara, Yokoo, Aoki, Inamura, Kakusho, Oshio, Sugiki, Ono, Fukumoto, Okajima, etc., who have been newly transferred from Tokyo, will take turns to provide armed protection, and the Marine Corps Headquarters will send 20 armed Marine Corps soldiers to each cargo ship to assist; (3) For goods shipped from the country to Shanghai, the Marine Corps Headquarters may, according to the situation, protect the safe unloading of the goods when reporting to customs for unloading. After the above four measures were deemed satisfactory by various Japanese commercial organizations in Shanghai, they were implemented the day before yesterday. As a result, the Yangtze River Maru of the Nisshin Shipping Company still loaded a large batch of Japanese goods worth about 800,000 yuan when it sailed to Hankou the day before yesterday, transporting them to the Yangtze River Estuary for unloading, including 60 boxes in Wuhu, 35 boxes in Jiujiang, 20 boxes in Yichang, and the most in Wuhan, about 100 boxes.

However, as a result of the discussion, in addition to recommending representatives to petition the consul stationed in Shanghai, requesting the municipal government to strictly prohibit it, there are no other practical measures. Public Statements from Various Trade Associations Regarding Abolishing the Tael and Changing to the Yuan 108

▲ General Agreement on Principles

▲ But Emphasis on New Currency and Paper Money

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce considers the abolition of the tael and change to the yuan to be of great importance. It previously sent a letter to Mr. Chen Xing, Deputy Governor of the Central Bank, inquiring about three points: (1) the weight and fineness of the new currency, (2) the method of converting taels to yuan, and (3) how to ensure public understanding. A circular was sent to various industries in the city to solicit opinions. In addition to the sugar industry and over ten other trade associations that have already expressed their views on these three points, as previously reported, the Chamber has now received replies from nine more trade associations, including the silk and satin industry. Key points are summarized below:

▲ Silk and Satin Industry: At a time when prices are falling and industry and commerce are suffering hidden losses, this policy is particularly urgent and a crucial plan that cannot be delayed. However, in all things there are often advantages and disadvantages. Before promoting benefits, it is essential to eliminate drawbacks. The crux of the disorder in our country's currency system lies in the lack of uniformity in prices and circulation. The Association believes that the abolition of the tael and change to the yuan is intended to unify the currency system. During implementation, three practical preparations must be made: (1) The fineness of the new currency, the decimal system, and all uses nationwide must be unified. (2) The fineness of coins must not be lower than the current weight. Coinage must be absolutely open and verifiable. (3) The issuance of paper money should have substantial reserves, absolutely guaranteed, and must not be suspended for redemption.

▲ Chinese Medicine Industry: (1) All provincial mints should be abolished simultaneously, and coinage should be exclusively under the Central Mint. Only then can the right to mint currency be unified, and the important weights and fineness of the new currency will not vary. (2) The right to issue paper money by all ordinary banks should be abolished simultaneously and uniformly, and be exclusively under the Central Bank. The banknotes should not have place names printed on them and should be exchangeable and redeemable everywhere.

▲ Western Paint Industry: (1) The weight and fineness of the new currency should follow the regulations of the currency system of the Third Year of the Republic. Trade groups should be convened to form a committee to supervise the implementation or conduct periodic verification, and the results should be reported and publicly announced. (2) The conversion of silver taels involves national debts and obligations. Chambers of commerce in various regions should be responsible for convening various industries to impartially and moderately stipulate rates or adopt the average silver price from the 18th, 19th, 20th, and 23rd years of the Republic as the legal price. (3) For unified issuance, a special treasury should be established, and the reserve fund should be in accordance with legal requirements, with at least 60% in cash. No other types of funds should be used for substitution, and it must be subject to public inspection by legal organizations at any time.

▲ Taxi Industry: (1) The new currency must have a moderate value. (2) The conversion ratio should be publicly stipulated. (3) The issuance reserve should be strictly inspected.

▲ Ice Fresh Fish Industry: The Association believes that if the government wants to rectify the currency system, it should start with reorganizing coins and paper money. Its proposals are as follows: (1) When minting new silver coins, all old coins circulating in the market must be uniformly withdrawn.

It is Most Important that the New Currency's Supply and Demand Correspond, The People Throughout the Country Must Have the Right to Supervise Coinage. (2) To reorganize paper money, a special bureau should be established with the right to unified issuance, and the reserve must be legal. Paper money not issued by the special bureau should be abolished. With legal reserves, inspections will be easy to carry out. (3) If the above two items can be implemented, the abolition of the tael and change to the yuan will be easily resolved. As for how to convert taels to yuan, chambers of commerce in various regions should be responsible for moderately stipulating rates based on the circumstances.

▲ Cotton Yarn Industry: The Association did not list specific opinions but generally agreed with the letter from the money exchange industry to Mr. Chen Xing and Mr. Ma Ji-liang's written opinions, and deeply admired Mr. Yu Qiaqing's telegram, considering it a deeply experienced view.

▲ Paper Industry: (1) The lack of uniformity in our country's coins, paper money, and subsidiary coins is just like the complexity of silver taels. Therefore, if the abolition of the tael and change to the yuan does not start from unifying the currency system, the effect will be minimal. A joint research committee should convene economic experts and industrial and commercial leaders from various provinces to discuss the crux of the matter, so that the entire currency system can be truly unified. (2) After the abolition of the tael and change to the yuan, all silver dollars will be used. Will all the previous premiums, appreciation, and water deductions still exist? (3) International trade has always converted using silver taels. After the abolition of the tael and change to the yuan, how can the new currency become the standard for the international trade currency system? (4) When using the new and old currencies, the old currencies should be gradually withdrawn. If the weight of the new currency is lower than the old currency, it is difficult to guarantee that unscrupulous people will not privately melt them down. If so, the value of the old silver coins will inevitably exceed the new currency. Although the government can easily withdraw them, the difference between the coinage cost and the silver color will inevitably increase the national treasury's expenditure. Is there any preparation for this? (5) When silver dollars are used together, most of the reserves are provided with sufficient silver (i.e., silver ingots). After the abolition of the tael and change to the yuan, the value of silver will naturally exist. Will silver ingots still be used for reserves in the future?

▲ Rickshaw Industry: The Association only focuses on Mr. Chen Xing's second principle, because all large and small shops have considerable contracts with the silver and money industry. If the foreign exchange rates are not stipulated first, disputes will continue. As long as this item is handled properly, there will be no social objections. As for the weight, fineness, and legal price of the new currency, the currency regulations of advanced countries in the East and West should be followed, and the currency should be minted according to the actual values. It must also be supervised and verified by various industry groups to ensure uniformity.

▲ Mr. Xian Xiang: (1) The weight and fineness of the new currency should have certain regulations, and the public and organizations should be allowed the right to supervise. (2) The exchange rate between silver taels and silver dollars should solicit opinions from all relevant parties to determine an impartial method. (3) Unified issuance to seek financial consolidation and dispel social doubts.

Japanese Person Returning from the United States Discusses American Public Opinion Towards Japan 110

▲ Stimulated by the Manchurian and Shanghai Incidents

The Japanese-language Shanghai Daily News reported that American public opinion towards Japan suddenly changed, triggered by the Shanghai Incident. During the Manchurian Incident, national public opinion was roughly divided into 60% pro-Japanese and 40% anti-Japanese. After the Shanghai Incident, the attitude suddenly changed, becoming 60% anti-Japanese, 20% neutral, and 20% pro-Japanese. Secretary of State Stimson's statements often revealed a threatening tone towards Japan, resulting in an extremely hardened public opinion towards Japan. As a result, rumors circulated that relations between Japan and the United States were in a precarious state. The reason for this was attributed to the stimulation of the American people by Chinese propaganda. Mr. Yamamoto Minezo, who returned from studying in the United States, came to Shanghai to inspect the Shanghai Incident and Chinese politics. He made the following remarks to reporters: Stimson's anti-Japanese remarks created anti-Japanese public opinion among Americans. Some intellectuals, such as professor groups at universities like Washington, Columbia, and Yale, even promoted economic disengagement with a "defeat Japan" doctrine due to the Manchurian Incident. Shortly after, the Shanghai Incident broke out, and the anti-Japanese sentiment expanded, increasingly believing that Japan was invading China. Although American pastors and local news provided explanations, the preconceived Chinese propaganda had already been imprinted in the minds of Americans. (Omission) As for the talk of a Japanese-American war, it was nothing more than what yellow newspapers in the same camp as Japan were promoting. Currently, the major problems in the United States are focused on countermeasures against the Communist Party and the unemployed.

Case of Chinese Man Arrested by Indian Constable in the Concession: Autopsy Reveals Injuries 113

Zhou A-yu (also known as Zhou A-you), a native of Shaoxing, was moving his stall and was stabbed to death and his third son stabbed and injured by Indian constables and others. The perpetrators, Sha- Sha Mengen and Ala Dat, were extradited to the British Consulate. On the morning of the 4th, the case was heard by British Consulate adjudicator Hams. The Public Security Bureau dispatched Qu Sunyi, an assistant from the Third Section, along with patrolman Wang Yan from the Third Precinct of the Fifth District, and Dong Wushi, the second landlord of the deceased Zhou A-yu, and witness Xu Junchuan, as well as blood-stained clothing and other evidence. After the trial, the defendant's lawyer requested that personnel from the Public Works Department be sent to the scene of the incident to investigate in detail and to examine how the deceased died to clarify the truth. The British Consulate issued a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Police, which was hand-delivered to Qu Sunyi, the representative of the Public Security Bureau, for joint examination. Director Wen sent a letter appointing forensic doctor Wei Ligong to conduct a joint examination with British doctor Beiden from the Public Works Department. They went to the Shaoxing Guild Hall in Zhabei at 5:30 PM on the 5th to open the coffin for examination. Yesterday, the Public Security Bureau reported on the report from forensic doctor Wei Ligong. The original letter states roughly: "According to your bureau's request, [I] was asked to conduct a joint examination with the Public Works Department doctor at the Shaoxing Guild Hall in Zhabei. [I] immediately went with Doctor Bei, two Chinese and Western detectives from the Huishan Police Station, and two gentlemen from your bureau, Qu and He, to open the coffin for examination. [We] found that Zhou A-yu (also known as Zhou A-you), aged 26, died of injuries on the 2nd of this month and was sent to the Guild Hall after being embalmed on the 3rd. [Examination] found that he was 1.65 meters tall, his clothes were intact, but after undressing, the entire body had begun to decompose. On the left chest, one inch above the left nipple, and two inches to the left of the left nipple, in between the fourth and fifth ribs, there was a horizontal wound about one inch long. The lung protruded from the wound. Because of decomposition, no other wounds were seen on the rest of the body. It was determined that he was stabbed in the left lung and died from the stab wound. Accordingly, [I] am reporting this." It is reported that the Public Security Bureau has solid evidence in the case and is now negotiating with the British Consulate based on the facts. Yesterday, the British Consulate's transmission of witness testimony has not yet ended.

Judgment in Chen Xing's Marital Dispute 114

Ordered to Compensate Yan Shufen 50,000 Yuan

Chen Xing, Deputy Governor of the Central Bank, engaged Miss Yan Shufen, a relative of Yan Dunyuan, the former Minister of Internal Affairs, as his wife when he was not yet successful. He also received repeated cultivation from his wife's family, who subsidized his tuition fees. However, while studying in the United States, Chen suddenly married a woman surnamed Cai, disregarding Miss Yan. After returning to the country and serving in the banking industry, he neither prepared to fulfill the previous marriage contract nor legally dissolved it, leaving Miss Yan alone in an empty boudoir, wasting her youth. Until last year, this old maid was already forty-two years old and could hardly continue to delay. When Chen was honored with the high position of Deputy Governor of the National Bank, she requested that Chen quickly resolve this ill-fated relationship. Because he refused to negotiate, the woman filed a complaint with the First Special District Local Court, requesting that the defendant be ordered to pay 100,000 yuan in damages for the loss caused by the delayed fulfillment of the marriage contract. During the trial, the defendant claimed that Yan Shufen had already married Fu Wutui, the nephew of the former Shanghai Daoyin Fu Jiang, in Beiping, so he could no longer marry her. The judge then ruled against the plaintiff. However, Yan Shufen swore that Chen's claims were false. Lawyer Yan Jiangyi filed an appeal with the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court and described in detail the marital relationship with Fu Wutui, stating that because Chen had delayed fulfilling the marriage contract and repeatedly wanted to dissolve the engagement, the elders of the family arranged a marriage with Fu Jiang's nephew through matchmakers such as Chen and Erren'an. However, she herself was familiar with female virtues and could not marry two husbands. Therefore, when the bridal sedan arrived, she resolutely cut her hair to show her determination. Now, Chen not only failed to understand her feelings but also falsely accused her, so she requested the court to revoke the original judgment and conduct an impartial investigation. She also tried to invite Fu Wutui to Shanghai. After the Second Branch of the High Court summoned him to testify, both lawyers debated in court and yesterday morning, Hu Yigu, the presiding judge of the civil court, along with Han and Ye, the two judges, announced the judgment. The main text read: "The original judgment is revoked. Chen Xing is ordered to compensate Yan Shufen 50,000 yuan. The appellant's remaining requests are rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne equally by both parties."

The Pearl Returns to Hepu 115

▲ Zhao Kaicai Intends to Adopt a Son

▲ Song Dalou Unintentionally Meets His Real Parent

The China Child Welfare Association rescued a child named Song Dalou in June 1931. According to him, he was a native of Tianjin, twelve years old, and was abused by his father. He escaped in the meantime and secretly boarded a transport ship to Shanghai to find his sister. After arriving on shore, he got lost and was almost abducted by villains. He was rescued by the Child Welfare Association and handed over to the Child Welfare Training Institute for education. This year, Zhao Kaicai, a bailiff from the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, a native of Hunan, nearly fifty years old, whose wife died ten years ago, leaving behind a son who was just two years old. He raised him until he was six years old, when he was suddenly abducted by bandits and could not be found despite searching everywhere. Now that he is nearly fifty and has no children, he asked Hu Yigu (also an executive member of the Association), the presiding judge of the civil court, to introduce him to the Training Institute of the Association to adopt an orphan as a son to comfort his loneliness. After the Association investigated and found him qualified, he was allowed to adopt a child. Zhao Kaicai went to the Institute a few days ago to choose and, upon seeing Song Dalou, seemed touched and said, "This child looks very much like my son who was lost six years ago." However, my son has a special birthmark on his back. Please check it in person. He immediately asked the child to take off his clothes to check, and indeed there was a birthmark, which matched what Zhao said. So, this child was Zhao's son who was lost six years ago. How he was abducted to Tianjin and then escaped to Shanghai, was rescued and educated by the Child Welfare Association, and finally allowed the pearl to return to Hepu and the family to reunite, although it was due to a miraculous coincidence, the work of the Child Welfare Association cannot be erased.

Female Corpse Found on Route Tenant de Vermale 116

▲ West of St. Mary's Hall

▲ Stab Wounds on Left Side of Neck and Chest

Yesterday (the 6th) at around 1:00 PM, a female corpse was suddenly discovered next to the road west of St. Mary's Hall on Route Tenant de Vermale. A passerby saw it and reported it to the Second Branch of the Sixth District Precinct in Zhoujiaqiao, which forwarded the report to the Sixth District Police Department. After receiving the report, the district chief immediately sent Inspector Xu to investigate. It was found that the nameless female corpse was about 50 years old, wearing blue cloth trousers, white gauze socks, and blue cloth shoes, and her hair was styled in a bun, resembling a local woman. There were stab wounds on the left side of her neck and chest, each very deep, with blood flowing profusely. It seemed that she was murdered and her body moved and abandoned here. After completing the investigation, the district chief reported back and ordered Xu Youyuan, the fourth-district bailiff in charge, to report to the local court for an autopsy. The court appointed Inspector Yang to bring a forensic official to the scene for examination. It was found that the deceased had indeed been stabbed to death with a knife while alive. As no family members were found to claim the body, it was ordered to report to the authorities to prepare a coffin and collect the body, pending the arrest and interrogation of the murderer.

Eurasia Aviation Corporation Prepares for Mail to Europe 119

▲ Full Line Expected to Open in Mid-October

After the termination of postal service between China and the East, mail originally transferred to Europe via the Siberian Railway was reloaded onto transport ships and transported to Europe by sea, which was very inconvenient. Xiong Shihui Explains the Reasons for the Special Goods Production and Sales Donation 123

▲ Reply to the Jiangxi Public Association Telegram

Xiong Shihui's reply to the Jiangxi Public Association telegram reads: "To the directors of the Shanghai Jiangxi Public Association, I have read the telegram from Ge Ri, expressing concerns about the recently implemented bandit suppression and rehabilitation donation in Jiangxi Province. Your concern for our homeland is the hallmark of benevolence, and I dare not but express my gratitude. However, Jiangxi is the area most severely affected by the Red scourge. In recent years, villages have been reduced to ruins, people have been displaced, and the Red bandits continue to use their communist heresies to collude with peasants, intoxicate the youth, and implement a predatory land policy. Crisis is looming and threatening to break. In this most difficult and critical period, it is necessary to identify goals, stride forward with a broad vision, and advance military and political affairs simultaneously, with a precise timeline, to achieve a fundamental solution. Quick fixes and temporary measures will not suffice. As the unworthy governor of my homeland, I am deeply concerned and, without overestimating myself, consider the elimination of banditry and the construction of

the region as my inescapable responsibility. Today, the key to governance in Jiangxi must be to strengthen our self-defense forces to prevent the attacks and movements of the Red bandits, avoid attacking the strong and attacking the weak, and prevent them from using the countryside as a base. It is also necessary to thoroughly measure land, reorganize land taxes, determine tenancy rights, and improve land rents, to destroy their poisonous plot of plundering and deceiving the peasants. Furthermore, establishing a security system to clarify household registration and repairing roads to facilitate transportation are also urgent measures. Jiangxi Province has always been known for its poverty, and the central government's assistance has been suspended since last December, resulting in a monthly reduction of 125,000 yuan. The tax revenue collected by various counties averages no more than 50%, and other miscellaneous income is also limited. The provincial treasury is so strained, and yet so many government affairs are waiting to be addressed. If you were in my position, what would you do? Last year, when Generalissimo Chiang came to Jiangxi to oversee the military operations, the enormous military expenditures were borne by the national treasury. Even the expenses required for the political anti-banditry work of the party-government committees and their subordinate district branches were covered by allocations from the headquarters. The local government could reduce this burden. However, the situation is different now. How can we rely on the national treasury for subsidies? Moreover, the relief funds were raised by me at sea. Providing disaster relief and comforting the afflicted is an ancient virtue. However, I have never heard of raising funds for political projects. The financial circulation of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces still allows for borrowing, which is not feasible in Jiangxi, where industry and commerce are in decline. The only way to raise funds is through taxation, and taxes are of three types: land tax, salt tax, and goods tax. Jiangxi's rural economy has long been bankrupt, and peasants are abandoning cultivation. We are preoccupied with providing relief and cannot afford to increase land taxes or impose excessive levies. Therefore, the only way to address the land tax is to strive to reorganize it, eliminate corruption, and then carry out measurement and determine land taxes to increase revenue. This has already begun in Nanchang, Xinjian, and Jinxian counties. The salt tax is a national tax. This spring, an additional surcharge of 1.5 yuan was added, which is expected to generate over 1.3 million yuan annually. Since its implementation, it has been relatively smooth. The tax revenue has been designated for road construction. The current bandit suppression and rehabilitation donation is the so-called goods tax. At the beginning of its implementation, we consulted widely and sought advice from many sources. All names, tax items, and collection methods were carefully considered to ensure the best possible outcome. Once the donation is paid, it is valid throughout the province, unlike the previous likin taxes, which involved setting up checkpoints at every stage. It cannot be considered harsh. It is only levied on a few major production and sales items, so it cannot be considered miscellaneous. Some commentators compare the abolition of likin with the imposition of donations. It should be understood that there is no absolute good or evil in politics, nor is there absolute right or wrong. It is about weighing the advantages and disadvantages and adapting to the times and circumstances. Today, what Jiangxi people are suffering from is the Communist bandits. They are worried day and night, and they cannot sleep or eat in peace. If bearing this donation enables the government to implement measures and achieve the goal of living and working in peace, I ask, will the people be happy to donate, or will they prefer to fold their hands and await slaughter by the Communist bandits? Therefore, the right and wrong, good and evil, of politics depend on the motive behind it. As for the benevolence of nurturing and the righteousness of loving one's children, I have doubts. The National Government's abolition of likin last year was indeed a good policy, but Hu Yongzhi's implementation of likin in the past was also not without its merits. If the Qing court had abolished likin as soon as the military suppression was completed in the early years of Tongzhi, it would only have seen its benefits and not its harms. When Hu was appointed governor of Hubei, Wuchang had just fallen, and the damage had not yet been repaired. He followed the example of Yangzhou and levied likin on merchants' goods, trying to equalize donations. Even the smallest items were contested. He took money from the merchants in Hankou and from the county property taxes to support the military expenses. At the same time, he requested the exemption of land taxes in 46 prefectures and counties, including Jiangxia, to relieve the people's hardship. The following year, he requested the reorganization of the grain tribute, reducing surcharges and eliminating redundant expenses, completely reforming the centuries-old malpractice. During the period of bandit suppression, the first priority is to protect farmers and facilitate commerce. In Jiangxi's recent experience, although we benefited from the abolition of likin last year, the situation of industry and commerce did not improve, but rather declined daily. This is because the bandit atmosphere is not quelled, and transportation has not been restored. Although taxes and likin have been reduced, their effect is minimal. Moreover, this production and sales donation was approved by the bandit suppression conference. The representatives of the conference were elected by the public law groups of various counties, who understood the local situation and believed that without bandit suppression, there could be no industry and commerce. They resolutely approved it and considered it feasible. I was still afraid of repeating the mistake of likin, which was established and never abolished. To prevent problems before they arise, I changed the name of the production and sales tax in the original proposal of the Finance Department to "Special Goods Production and Sales Bandit Suppression and Rehabilitation Donation," which is entirely based on Jiangxi's special circumstances, using the local people's donations to address local urgent needs. This is the humble effort of me and my colleagues that I hope you will understand. The estimated annual revenue from the production and sales donation is only over two million yuan, most of which must be used for bandit suppression and rehabilitation needs. The amount that can be used to increase the security guard teams is only over 900,000 yuan, which is far from the expected amount. It can be seen that it cannot be used exclusively to increase eight regimental units. However, considering the current situation in Jiangxi, if we can add these eight regiments, it may not be a misfortune for the region. Given the current financial difficulties, I dare not hope for its realization. Therefore, the budget for the 21st year only allocates 930,000 yuan as the minimum increase. I ask myself, my heart is clear and I am not ashamed before heaven and earth. You are far away on the coast, and you may not be familiar with the true situation in your homeland. You may be misled by one or two merchants who do not understand the overall situation and spread rumors, resulting in accusations. I have no choice but to lay bare my heart and analyze the advantages and disadvantages before you. I came here solely for the sake of saving Jiangxi. I am willing to go through fire and water for anything that benefits the region. I have never cared about right or wrong, praise or slander. It is easy to please those who are good in the homeland, but difficult to avoid the dislike of those who are not. As for the accusation that I am expanding the teams for ulterior motives, although I am unworthy, I have led tens of thousands of troops to quell the chaos. If I were to insist on owning several regimental units to establish my chieftain's and chieftain's power, then what could move my heart? In the past, Hu Yongzhi's memorial requesting the reorganization of the grain tribute stated, "If it benefits the country, if it benefits the people, then I will not hesitate to sing the song of slaughter." Those who do good are the happiest, and only those who are selfless are strong. It is easy to talk about things in the world, but difficult to do them. It takes a hundred years to build, but one word can destroy it. You are all elders of your homeland, respected by all. I hope you will understand the difficulties of the times and work together in the same boat. Jiangxi's troubles are deep, and Jiangxi's people are suffering. Today's affairs, even if the entire Jiangxi people work together, it is still difficult to hope for success. How can we create side issues and cause further disputes? I believe that those who love their homeland would not do this. I hope you will consider and understand. Jiangxi will be fortunate. Xiong Shihui, winter seal."

The Two National Goods Associations Request Negotiations Regarding the A.P. Earle Light Bulb Case 124

The Shanghai Citizens' National Goods Promotion Association and the China National Goods Maintenance Association's member, A.P. Earle Electrical Factory's light bulbs, were sued by the Philips Company in the Batavia court. Details were reported in yesterday's newspaper. Yesterday, the two national goods associations sent a telegram to Consul Song in Java, requesting the Chinese Chamber of Commerce in Java to argue based on reason. Telegrams were sent to the Central Party Headquarters, the Executive Yuan of the National Government, the Ministry of Industry, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, requesting serious negotiations. They also sent letters to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, the Overseas Chinese Federation, and other organizations, requesting them to assist in safeguarding national rights and maintaining national goods. The original telegram reads: (Headings omitted) "According to a letter from our member, A.P. Earle Electrical Factory, our factory's various types of light bulbs have been sold both domestically and internationally for many years, especially in Southeast Asia. This has caused jealousy among the colonial powers. In February of this year, the Dutch Philips Light Bulb Company, claiming that the "haff bubble" (i.e., argon bubble) was invented by their company and enjoys a patent, prohibited the Dutch East Indies General Agency Batavia Youth Trading Company from selling our factory's haff bubbles. We had to stop selling under duress. Unexpectedly, the Philips Company was not satisfied and wanted to completely defeat all brands of light bulbs on the market to implement a monopoly plan. Seeing that the style and quality of our factory's light bulbs were comparable to their products, they deliberately wanted to defeat us first, claiming that the method of using glass tubes to extract air from the light bulbs was also their invention and infringed on their patent rights. They sued us in the local court, demanding compensation. The Youth Company, which was selling the goods, had to pay local tariffs when the goods arrived, so they returned the original 23 boxes of our factory's newly shipped light bulbs. At the same time, they hired famous lawyers to defend us when the time comes. The method of extracting air from glass tubes is commonly used in various light bulbs today. We have never heard that it was invented and patented by Philips. Now, they are fabricating excuses to crack down on us and implement a monopoly. It is nothing more than bullying our country for being weak and unable to protect overseas Chinese, arbitrarily slaughtering us, and infringing on our commerce. Accordingly, we request that you provide relief and protect overseas trade, etc." After the meeting, it was found that the glass tube air extraction method is a necessary procedure for manufacturing light bulbs. The Philips Company is jealous of the wide sales of A.P. Earle light bulbs and regards them as a strong enemy. They are using the excuse of patents to deliberately defeat us, sparing no effort to destroy and invade us. If this precedent is set, the loss of part of the factory's business is a small matter, but the future of national goods in overseas trade is no small matter. Moreover, our country's science is backward, and the production of national goods is mostly based on imitation of foreign machines. Southeast Asia is the base area for our country's national goods to be sold overseas. It poses a great danger to overseas Chinese merchants who promote national goods. Our association advocates national goods and promotes trade. We cannot remain silent. In addition to telegraphing the Consul General in Java and the Chinese Chamber of Commerce in Java to argue based on reason and provide assistance, we specially request that you safeguard national goods in overseas trade, protect overseas Chinese merchants, and promote national goods. Please conduct serious negotiations as soon as possible to safeguard national rights and maintain national goods. (Omissions below) Wang Jie'an, Wang Hanqiang, and Wang Xingyi, Standing Committee Members of the China National Goods Maintenance Association; Yu Hede, Feng Shaoshan, Chen Yiting, Chen Binghui, Fang Jiange, Xu Jianruo, and Zhang Dezhai, Standing Committee Members of the Shanghai Citizens' National Goods Promotion Association, respectfully kowtow, fish seal.

Ministry of Communications Telecommunications Factory Installs Beijing-Shanghai Wireless Telephone 126

▲ Radio station to be set up in Zhenru

Since the National Government established its capital in Nanjing, transportation between Beijing and Shanghai has become increasingly busy. In the event of urgent incidents, it is extremely inconvenient to rely solely on wired long-distance telephones. Yu Ruxin, director of the Telecommunications Machinery Manufacturing Factory of the Ministry of Communications, in order to facilitate rapid transportation between Beijing and Shanghai, is preparing to establish a wireless telephone direct to Nanjing. According to Yu, speaking to a reporter from the East China News Agency, the entire plan had been drafted in advance. The factory will manufacture two radio stations themselves, which will cost approximately 30,000 yuan. The Shanghai station will be set up in Zhenru, with an antenna reaching the Sassoon Building radio station. Anti-Opium Society Advocates Thorough Investigation of the Military Counselor's Office Smuggling Case 127

The China National Anti-Opium Society believes that the discovery of the Military Counselor's Office smuggling soil has caused a public outcry and has had a significant impact on the future of opium prohibition. It has sent a letter to Chairman Lin of the National Government, advocating a thorough investigation. The original letter is transcribed below: [Dear Sir, According to recent reports in the Beijing-Shanghai newspapers, at the Nanjing Xiaguan Railway Station, military police uncovered five large boxes of smuggled opium soil being privately transported by Section Chief Xiao of the Military Counselor's Office of the National Government, all affixed with seals from the Military Counselor's Office of the National Government. After the incident was discovered, he claimed that it belonged to Military Counselor Lu Chao and that he was not responsible. This is extremely shocking. Smuggling opium soil is a violation of criminal law. The Military Counselor's Office is a high-level agency of the National Government, and the Military Counselor is a senior military and political official. They are entrusted with the dignity of the government and the attention of the international community. How can they disregard national law, violate criminal law, and compete with opium dealers for petty profits, disgracing the national image? There is nothing worse than this. It is heard that after the incident, Lu claimed that it was done by his subordinates and that he was not responsible. In the past, in many cases of important figures transporting soil, they all pushed the blame onto their subordinates. For example, in the Jiang'an transport ship opium smuggling case of the previous year, everyone knew the background, and the result was also to push the blame onto the subordinates, letting them off lightly. The important figures who instigated and escorted the smuggling were able to escape punishment. Finally, there was an even more unexpected outcome: those who sheltered the opium smugglers were promoted, while those who investigated the opium smugglers were dismissed. Public justice and national law were completely destroyed. This is deeply regrettable. This time, the Military Counselor's Office is again smuggling soil and claiming that it was done by subordinates. How can the story be exactly the same? Moreover, Chinese soldiers transporting soil has become a commonplace fact, such as warships escorting and airplanes transporting. There are countless examples. Therefore, the Military Counselor's Office privately transporting opium is truly impossible for people not to suspect. However, in the past, most of the cases involved local soldiers. Now, even the central senior agency, the Military Counselor's Office, is known for transporting soil. The magnitude of the matter and the importance of the relationship cannot be compared. Moreover, the occurrence of this case comes immediately after the central government reiterated the opium prohibition. The senior officials of the Military Counselor's Office knowingly violated the law and took the lead. It is truly unknown what they were thinking. Furthermore, the case of Gao Ying and his wife, the former deputy consul in San Francisco, smuggling opium soil, was dealt with severely by the authorities due to diplomatic relations. Even without diplomatic relations, the Military Counselor's Office transporting soil has sullied the international community and made us a laughingstock to the world. It is even more serious than the Gao case and should be thoroughly investigated and dealt with severely in order to maintain credibility and emphasize prohibition. I respectfully request that Your Excellency uphold impartiality, break through personal considerations, and investigate and handle the case according to law. Do not let one person be spared at the expense of a hundred, allowing the national administration to become increasingly corrupt and the trend of opium smuggling to never end. The party and the country will be fortunate, and the opium prohibition will be fortunate."]

Social Affairs Bureau Registers and Compiles Statistics on Foreign Rice and Foreign Wheat 128

The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau has been registering foreign rice and foreign wheat for more than a year. During the Shanghai War this year, many rice shops in Zhabei moved to the concessions. This registration was briefly suspended, but it was resumed in April. The bureau has repeatedly ordered various shops to comply with the reporting requirements. Therefore, the number of registered items is quite large. It is now known that the registration for July has been completed. A total of 8,000 bags of foreign rice were registered for order, 520,500 bags of foreign rice were registered for arrival, and 174,950 tons of foreign wheat were registered for arrival. Some rice shops, such as Yuantai and Wanshengxing, have not yet reported their arrival. The bureau has instructed the Rice Industry Association to instruct these shops to report by the 15th of this month.

Current Situation of Zhabei Porridge Distribution 129

▲ 1,680 registered numbers

▲ More than 3.5 dan of rice needed daily for porridge distribution

Wu Xingya, director of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, previously inspected the war zone and was extremely indignant at the devastation. He was especially saddened by the fact that most of Zhabei had been completely destroyed, leaving a scorched earth. He believed that after the war, most of the poor people had lost their homes and could not afford to eat. He immediately instructed the relevant departments to coordinate the reconstruction plan and paid special attention to the relief of the poor. He ordered Zhang Binghui, chief of the fourth section of the bureau, to formulate a porridge distribution plan. Zhang, citing the current municipal treasury expenditure, was unable to request funds. He submitted a request to the municipal government to allocate 3,000 yuan from the temporary relief fund and handed it over to Wang Binyan, director of the Zhabei Charity Association, to organize porridge distribution in the Liulu area. It officially opened on the 2nd of this month, distributing porridge every day from 5:00 AM to 7:00 AM. The director, to prevent abuse, notified the general public in advance that they must first register and receive a ticket before they could receive porridge. On the first day, there were more than 600 people. On the second and third days, there were more than 800 people. By the 4th, a total of 1,680 numbers had been registered.

Page 16

Although the deadline has passed, the amount of rice needed for porridge distribution every day is more than 3 dan and 5 dou. Those who did not register temporarily were also given leniency, and their formalities were waived. The weather is becoming cooler with the approach of autumn, and rain is expected soon. The porridge distribution shelter is inadequate and urgently needs to be expanded with reed mats, totaling more than 40 square meters in two places. Each square meter costs 5 yuan and 2 jiao, totaling more than 200 yuan, to prevent wind and rain. The matter has been submitted to the Social Affairs Bureau for review. The Social Affairs Bureau will send personnel to investigate and then approve the allocation. The bureau has also assigned staff members Cui Cong and Zhu Yulin to be responsible for inspecting everything at Liulu Road at any time.

The tour schedule is recorded below: (1) Balance distribution quality; (2) The chemistry department tests various water qualities such as tap water and natural water. After investigation and testing, it is confirmed that it is clean before notifying the Public Works Bureau that it can be used as drinking water; (3) The pharmacology department specializes in researching new drugs and is allowed to be released after testing; (4) Germ inspection, testing of patient size, typhoid fever, etc.; (6) The icebox room specializes in freezing serum and drug culture medium; (7) The vaccine manufacturing room, preventing meningitis, typhoid fever, cholera, etc.; (8) The rabies vaccine manufacturing room, preventing rabies bites, etc.; (9) The drying and disinfection room, such as glass instruments, is disinfected before storing objects; (10) The steam disinfection room and manufacturing laboratory, etc., are all explained in detail.
