Taxi Industry Association Advocates Exploitation of Our Country's Oil Mines 131

▲ Increase National Defense for the Country

▲ Seek Benefits for Colleagues

The Shanghai Taxi Industry Association, after its 29th executive committee meeting, decided to seek the opinions of all colleagues regarding the exploitation of oil mines. Yesterday, the association sent a special letter to its colleagues, stating: "Dear Sir, In our letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce on June 20th regarding the promotion of national goods and the establishment of industry, we failed to mention the exploitation of oil mines, which is a regrettable omission. It is believed that the main reason why the Japanese are actively plotting to take over the Northeast is that they want to obtain an oil-producing area. They fear that if a second world war breaks out and the sea routes are inevitably blockaded, the supply of gasoline will be cut off because the three islands do not have such production. Therefore, even if they have a large number of aircraft, it will be as if they do not have them. Therefore, the tighter the situation among the great powers, the more urgently the Japanese are plotting. It is found that our country has oil-producing areas in Jilin in the Northeast, Shanxi and Shaanxi in the Northwest, and Sichuan and Guangxi in the Southwest. If we want to defend against foreign insults and develop transportation, then advocating the exploitation of oil mines is an urgent task. For this reason, we request that your association forward this to the Ministry of Industry and request that it promulgate protection regulations, and send technicians and mining engineers to visit various places. At the same time, we request the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce to send inquiries to the local municipal chambers of commerce for detailed investigation, and solicit reports from local residents, so that they can be collected and considered before planning the capital and engaging in separate exploitation, which is an important item for the country's defense equipment, and a lifeline for our industry's daily consumption. It will benefit both the country and the merchants. We propose our humble opinions and request that they be adopted and implemented." After this was sent, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce replied that it had telegraphed the Ministry of Industry regarding the exploitation of oil mines, requesting that it be reviewed and implemented. Now, we have received approval document Mining Character No. 5804, stating that the exploitation of oil mines is an important political affair, and the Ministry had previously proposed to start exploiting the Shaanxi oil mines first, and has already planned and estimated the costs, which has been presented to the Central Political Conference and approved on record. However, due to lack of funds, it has not yet been implemented. The association is concerned about the oil mine industry, and its views are exactly the same as those of the Ministry. If the association can assist in the process, it will definitely achieve twice the result with half the effort. Please collect opinions and propose a method of raising large sums of money as soon as possible, and submit them for review. According to this, we have learned that our industry's daily consumption of gasoline has not been exploited in our country, and relies on the supply of imported goods, which are manipulated by foreign merchants, who arbitrarily raise and lower prices and do whatever they want. Their business competition is becoming increasingly fierce, and the rent is even more difficult to increase sharply. Once gasoline prices soar, we will inevitably be stuck waiting for death. Whenever we think of this, we feel chills down our spines. In order to prevent this from happening, this association is advocating the exploitation of oil mines in the country, which will increase national defense for the country and seek benefits for colleagues. There is nothing better than this. Fortunately, the Ministry of Industry's approval has been issued, but the plan for raising funds has not yet been achieved. It is believed that it is difficult to achieve success alone, but it is easy to lift with everyone. Therefore, we are specially requesting the assistance of the Automobile Industry Association and the Rubber Hardware and Auto Parts Industry Association, and corresponding inquiries are made to solicit the opinions of our colleagues and investment methods, so that we can collect and consider them comprehensively, collect and review them, and then report to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and forward them to the Ministry of Industry for implementation. It is believed that this matter is closely related to the interests of our colleagues, and we trust that you will agree. Please investigate and reply as soon as possible. We wish you all the best. Shanghai Taxi Industry Association."

▲ Dispute at the Welcoming of President Wang

The Shanghai Journalists Association received a letter yesterday from members Xu Shen and Wu Dong, which read: "To Whom It May Concern, President of the Executive Yuan Wang Jingwei arrived in Shanghai by special train. They learned that the special train would stop beside the freight station behind the Meigen Road freight station. Xu Shen and others drove there, arriving close to 5:00 AM. Chen then questioned how they knew President Wang was arriving in Shanghai, and ordered the railway police to use force to expel them. Xu Shen and others were about to explain everything to Chen when they were stopped by the railway police captain, who ordered them to leave. Shen and others, having reached their limit of tolerance, still explained everything politely, stating that interviewing was a journalist's freedom, and unless they were committing illegal acts, they should not be subjected to unreasonable expulsion and shouting. Chen became even angrier and took his anger out on the police officers, ordering them to ensure that the car Xu Shen and others were in was driven away and not allowed to park at the station. It was found that the place was next to the road, but it was a public road for people to travel on. How could he interfere arbitrarily? This was clearly an abuse of authority. However, Xu Shen and others, to avoid complications, still tolerated it and ordered the driver to drive the car away and wait. Later, Chen left on a locomotive, and drove the President's car to Zhenru. Xu Shen and others, due to their duty to investigate the news, had Wu Dong wait at the original station, while Xu Shen took a car back to Zhenru. Unexpectedly, Chen still did not understand in Zhenru and continued to order the railway police to block Xu Shen from entering the station and arbitrarily insulted him. These barbaric actions disregard the personality of reporters. To protect the dignity of all reporters and to facilitate future work, Xu Shen has written this letter to inform you of the situation and hopes that you will seriously negotiate with the bureau chief to ensure that the above-mentioned matters do not happen again."

Animal Husbandry Expert He Liyuan Returns to China 136

▲ Bringing Twenty Milk Cows

Animal husbandry expert Dr. He Liyuan has lived in the Americas for twenty-six years. He has profound research and experience in animal husbandry, especially in raising cattle. Recently, he has realized that his motherland needs to develop industry to enrich people's lives. He specially selected twenty of the purest breeds of milk cows from the Americas and transported them back to China to start improving the rural economy. Dr. He is from Xinhui, Guangdong. He studied in the Americas in his early years, and then engaged in business in the United States, engaged in the cattle raising industry, for a total of twenty-six years. He lived in Kansas City in the central United States and slightly placed real estate. He collected the best American breeds of cattle on his own farm for practical experiments, and the results were excellent. His deeds have been repeatedly published in American animal husbandry magazines, and he has won the reputation of an American cattle breeder. Therefore, people from all countries in the United States know Dr. He. His being elected as a member of the North American Society of Animal Science is also for this reason. This is the first Chinese person to join the association, and he has won a lot of glory for the country. Dr. He returned to China three months ago. At that time, Shanghai had just experienced war and order had not been restored, so he specially transported his cattle to Hong Kong for temporary residence to avoid danger. Now that Shanghai has gradually calmed down, he has transported the cattle to Shanghai a few days ago and plans to live there for a long time. He is currently surveying locations and contacting personnel to prepare for the construction of a cattle farm. Dr. He's resolute return to China with cattle this time is purely driven by patriotism. He deeply feels that living overseas for a long time contributes little to the motherland, and he should do more production work for the motherland in the future. His friends in Shanghai, such as Chuan Ruoyu, Wu Wenwei, Tang Wenti, Li Jin, and Cheng Shao, admire his ambition and believe that his work is of great importance to the national economy and people's livelihood, and are willing to do their best to help him succeed.

Grinding Stone Burst - Autopsy of Yang Renlong's Tragic Death 140

Yang Renlong, a local man, 16 years old, was a worker at the Rui Rong Iron Factory on Yangshupu Road. At about 9 AM the day before yesterday, while he was grinding a steel plate, the grinding stone suddenly burst, and the gravel flew around, injuring Yang. At that time, Yang was seriously injured and fell unconscious. Later, his companion Yuan Rongquan caught a glimpse of it and immediately reported to the factory owner, who took him to the Sacred Heart Hospital for treatment in a car. The treatment was ineffective, and he died soon after. The hospital reported to the Yulin Road Police Station, which ordered detectives to investigate. The body was then moved to the Filun Road Autopsy Station. Yesterday morning, the First Special District Court was reported to dispatch Prosecutor Guo Wei, along with forensic doctor Zhang Yan and clerk Wang Zuyi, etc., to the station to examine the body. The autopsy was publicly opened. Yuan Rongquan reported that the deceased and I were both workers in the factory. At that time, he was injured by the bursting grinding stone, which I saw later. The grinding stone was made of four pieces of glue. It was rotating all day long. The deceased rubbed the steel plate that day, but the stone had been used for a long time, causing it to suddenly burst. The deceased's brother Yang Zhaolong reported that I did not see it at the time and requested the factory to give compensation. Mr. Guo obtained the confession and then announced that the deceased Yang Renlong had indeed died from his injuries before his death. The body was handed over to the deceased's brother Yang Zhaolong to sign a guarantee to take back the coffin for burial.

Apprentice Arson Case Judgment 141

Sentenced to One Year Imprisonment with Two Years Probation

Xu Yonglin, a native of Haimen, an 18-year-old apprentice at the Ri Xin Laundry Company at No. 2136 Peng Road, has been working at the company for three months. In the past, his conduct was not bad, but Xu suddenly got up from his bed at about 3 AM on the 2nd of this month, and poured a cup of gasoline on the paper box of clothes entrusted to the customer for washing in the store hall to set fire. His colleague apprentice Shen Gensen noticed it and worked with the boss, Chen Gaofeng from Ningbo, to put out the fire. Xu Yonglin was arrested by the Hongkou Police Station and sent to the First Special District Court. He confessed that he was haunted by nightmares and caused the disaster, seeking forgiveness. The interrogator ordered him to be detained for sentencing. As has been recorded in this newspaper, yesterday morning, Judge Shen Bingrong came to court and sentenced Xu Yonglin to one year of imprisonment with two years of probation for arson and destruction of other people's property. He also declared that he would instruct the defendant, considering that he was ignorant and pardonable, and that he must never do such a thing in his dreams again. The lawyer from the police station, Zhang, stated that during the appeal period, he should still be detained. The court approved it.

News of Gao You Township Association's Medical Assistance 146

The medical services of the Second Clinic of the Gao You Township Association in the East Shanghai District are developing rapidly. Because the original address is not enough, it has been expanded. Since the 25th of last month, it has moved to the new clinic at No. 24 Mingde Li, Songpan Road for consultation. The director of the clinic, Zheng Xiaobo, hired two doctors, She Shuqing and Luo Yunzhang, as assistants, and two good men from the same township, Xue Minggui and Jiang Dexing, donated funds to be responsible for the clinic's medication.

Newly Issued Maps of Two Routes 147

The area between Nanjing, Shanghai and Hangzhou is Jiangnan, where are many famous tourist attractions. The traffic on the two routes of Jinghu and Huhang is particularly busy. The Rixin Cartography Agency on Albert Road in Shanghai, recognizing the importance of travel maps, has produced and published a complete map of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo railway regions. Everything from the topography and transportation to the resources of the Jiangnan area is clear at a glance with this map. The mileage and number of days for transportation in various places are also noted, which is very suitable for travel. The stationery department of Wing On Company, China Travel Service, and various bookstores in Shanghai all have them for sale. The Shanghai and Nanjing maps published by the company are also very popular due to their accurate investigation.

Establishment of the "1932" Painting Studio 148

The White Goose Painting Research Institute, formerly located on North Sichuan Road in Shanghai, was founded by famous artists Chen Qiucao, Fang Xuegu, and Du Xuegu, Pan Sitong, etc. It has existed for many years and has long been praised by people in society. During the January 28th Shanghai Incident, the institute was located in the war zone and was tragically affected, being completely destroyed and sacrificed for the national crisis. As a result, existing researchers who wanted to continue their studies and those who aspired to art and wanted to join such a group lacked suitable places. The founders, seeing this, gathered teachers and students staying in Shanghai a few days ago and held a tea party at Guanshengyuan. More than 50 people attended the meeting.

It was decided to organize the 1932 Painting Studio to continue research. The address is temporarily set at M12 Xiangkang Li, Meibike Road. Research has already begun yesterday, divided into day and night departments, with complete equipment and low fees. It is now heard that new members will be recruited.

Wu Xing Xu Xiaonong Passes Away 150

Mr. Xu Xiaonong of Wu Xing was a famous official of the late Qing Dynasty. Since the revolution, he has lived in seclusion in Hubei Province, and later lived in Shanghai. He devoted himself to saving the world and alleviating poverty, providing medical treatment and medicine tirelessly, and never accepting rewards from others. He lived frugally all his life. At the age of sixty, he was still strong and had never been ill since his youth. This spring, he contracted a minor illness, but it was fatal. Mr. Xu passed away more than a month ago, but those who came to his door seeking medical treatment and medicine are still endless. His sons are all able to imitate his virtue, are benevolent, filial, and kind, and can carry on their father's will. They continue to provide medicine in the same way as their father, but they will only be able to continue after the major affairs are settled.

Letter Requesting the Stamp Tax Bureau to Return Account Books 151

The Shanghai Wine and Tea House Industry Association sent a letter to the Special District Stamp Tax Bureau, which reads: "To Whom It May Concern, according to a statement from our member, the Fairness Bureau First Floor Restaurant on Tangshan Road, Hongkou, on the morning of the 2nd of this month, the bailiffs came to the store and took away nine account books and draft books placed in our restaurant. At that time, it was said that failure to affix stamp tax violated the rules, etc. After investigation, the vouchers used by our store all have stamp tax affixed to the first page of the account books, and there is no intentional omission in violation of the regulations. However, although the vouchers are affixed for the 20th year, according to business customs, the account books and vouchers have not been used up, and they should continue to be valid for use in the following year. According to the regulations, one cent is affixed to each book. If it is affixed again, it will cause merchants to suffer intangible losses. Please send a letter to negotiate for the return, etc. After investigation, the penalty for failing to affix stamp tax should be based on those who do not affix it as negligence. Since the stamp tax has been affixed, the vouchers cannot be taken away and penalized for no reason. Therefore, this letter requests your bureau to quickly return the nine account books and vouchers of Gongping Yi Lou to avoid losses and maintain the hardship of business. It is reasonable to inform you and hope you will investigate and reply. (Omitted below)"

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday said that the Yangtze River basin is hot and cloudy, the Shandong Sea Road coast and the rest of the coast are Hu southeast winds, the wind in the Taiwan Strait comes from various directions ranging from northeast to northwest, and the weather in southeastern Taiwan is bad because a hurricane in the Pacific Ocean is moving northwest, its center had advanced to within 120 miles of the intersection of 18 degrees north latitude and 128 degrees east longitude at about 2 PM, the wind force is unknown. Also, within 24 hours before 3 PM yesterday, the local temperature was 99.3 degrees at its highest and 77.0 at its lowest. The highest was 93.0 and the lowest was 76.1 on the same day last year.

Letters to the Editor 155

Esteemed Mr. Sheng Bi,

With deepest respects, we begin this letter. Our group, realizing the daily urgency of the national crisis and finding no way to die for our cause, has formed the "Blood Soul Exterminate Traitors Group." We hope to awaken the deadened hearts of the people through the sacrifice of our blood and souls. On one hand, we aim to reduce the enemy's power of aggression by severing their economic lifelines. On the other hand, with pure patriotic aspirations, we strive for international peace. The Japanese ambition to violate treaties and invade the Northeast is largely due to the profits provided by our people's years of buying and selling Japanese goods. Therefore, those who remain unenlightened and continue to buy and sell Japanese goods today have committed the crime of harming the Republic by aiding foreign enemies against the nation and bear the responsibility of indirectly undermining international treaties. Hence, our group is issuing warnings to such individuals, hoping they will reform. Yesterday, while our member, Yun Huifang, was issuing a warning to the Maochang Foreign Goods Store, she was arrested by the police. Our comrades are determined to face any legal consequences with the spirit of "death before dishonor," but that is not what we fear. However, we believe it necessary to examine whether warning people to change their ways out of love for the nation and to uphold international peace constitutes a crime and what kind of legal punishment should be applied. We respectfully request that you publish this letter in your esteemed newspaper and initiate a "Legal Research Society for Exterminating Traitors," so that various public organizations and individuals who sympathize with our group can fully express their opinions. This will allow for a fair assessment of whether our members' actions constitute a crime and whether they should be subject to legal punishment. In addition to expressing our legal views separately at a later date, we send this letter in advance, wishing you well.

Sincerely,

Shanghai Blood Soul Exterminate Traitors Group

Red Blood Eliminate Traitors Group

August 6th, the twenty-first year of the Republic of China

Esteemed Mr. Editor of the Shen Bao,

Regarding the incident of our Blood Soul Exterminate Traitors Group leaving a bullet at your newspaper today, we respectfully present a brief outline of the events. Since late July, our store has received letters from both the Youth Iron Blood Group and the Blood Soul Exterminate Traitors Group. Yesterday morning, a youth came and delivered a hand grenade, followed by a letter from the Blood Soul Exterminate Traitors Group, warning us not to sell enemy goods and demanding that we publish a statement in the newspaper. All of us in this store share the patriotic heart of the Yanhuang people; how could we lag behind others? Although we unfortunately deal in cotton cloth, it was placed in the Anti-Japanese Association for safekeeping and only returned to us in April of this year. Our store, with its capital invested in this stock, has sold it gradually to alleviate our financial difficulties. We dare not be so heartless and insane as to import enemy goods on a large scale and resell them. The members of the Blood Soul Exterminate Traitors Group are all patriotic youths. We are sincerely gratified by their act of delivering a bullet as a warning. We deeply believe in the thoroughness of the Blood Soul Exterminate Traitors Group's organization. They even left a bullet as a warning regarding the sale of enemy goods purchased before September 18th, which had been sealed. They will certainly not easily forgive those who actually sell enemy goods. To ensure that enemy goods disappear, our store wishes to declare to all sectors with the utmost sincerity and blood-filled resolve that, even if it leads to closing our doors, we will never sell enemy goods again. With the national crisis becoming more urgent every day, our nation's last hope lies in the undying patriotism of the people. The colleagues at our store are willing to heed the warning of the Blood Soul Group and lay bare our hearts. We hope you will investigate and include this in the "Letters to the Editor" column. We wish you peace.

Sincerely,

The Colleagues of Yongyu Cloth Store

August 6th

With deepest respects, we begin this letter. Having read today's (August 6th) local news section of your esteemed newspaper, there is a news item titled "(National Salvation Ten-Person Group Joint Association Warns Three Ice and Seafood Shops in Nanshi)." It mentions that the association, based on secret reports, claims that our shop is selling fresh fish transported by Japanese ships. We are extremely surprised to read this. In addition to publishing a statement in the newspaper, we are writing this letter to request that your esteemed editor provide a correction and disclose this letter in the "Letters to the Editor" column, so that everyone is aware and any misunderstandings are cleared up. Special Article

How Should Students Utilize Summer Vacation? (II) 157

By Wang Xiaoying

(A) Regarding Character

(1) Traveling to famous mountains and rivers, cultivating a broad-minded spirit, shedding narrow local views, or other feudal sectarian views.

(2) Reading biographies and autobiographies of great inventors and all scholars, cultivating habits of hard work, perseverance, and a deep love for learning.

(3) Understanding the suffering of the people, developing a desire to improve society, and rejecting selfish desires.

(B) Regarding Willpower

(1) Recognizing the suffering of the entire nation under oppression, thus strengthening the determination to oppose imperialism.

(2) Reading biographies of great revolutionaries in the world, cultivating a spirit of self-sacrifice for the benefit of society.

C. Physical Training

Our people have always been ridiculed by foreigners as the "sick men of East Asia," and we are in a position of a weak nation, suffering the trampling of imperialism. The current situation is becoming increasingly dangerous. We must train our bodies so that we have the strength to defend ourselves and eventually become strong.

(A) Regarding Recreation

Such as the organization and competition of ball teams, practice of martial arts, practice and competition of swimming and boating, etc.

(B) Regarding Labor

Such as learning military training, hiking, participating in various family and social labor, etc.

D. Promoting Culture

The decline of rural culture is also a cause of national turmoil. Students are supported by society to study, and they should serve society as much as possible. If we wait until graduation to approach society, it will be a major mistake. We should strive to approach society on a regular basis so we can be students of society, not just living books or dictionaries.

The term "culture" encompasses a broad range, including customs, habits, religion, writing, etc. Our promotion should be divided into two aspects: propaganda and implementation. There is an inseparable connection between the two.

(A) Regarding Propaganda

Such as lectures on international situations and the Northeast issue, or personal conversations; suggestions on improving crops and irrigation methods, disaster prevention equipment, and eliminating pests; warnings about preventing epidemics; advocating afforestation, raising chickens, and raising carp in rice paddies; vigorously promoting literacy campaigns; breaking superstitions and bad habits, such as early marriage, drowning of female infants, clan fights, frivolous lawsuits, etc.; emphasizing public health, etc.

(B) Regarding Implementation

Such as the organization of sports associations, summer tutoring schools, mobile libraries, open-air schools, etc.; the establishment of temporary epidemic hospitals, catching and reducing pests, encouraging the implementation of public health, etc.

The above outlines are only general suggestions for what should be done. Students include elementary school students and university students, with vastly different abilities and knowledge. Therefore, each person should choose what they can do, first make a plan. Two points should be noted when creating a plan:

(1) Some parts of the plan must be done together with nearby classmates or local people. That part needs to be discussed with everyone, or after a meeting, and then the work you are responsible for should be added to your personal plan.

(2) The plan should not only specify what you should do, but also pay attention to the allocation of time. For example, use four-tenths of the time for academic research, two-tenths of the time for physical and mental cultivation, two-tenths of the time for physical training, and two-tenths of the time for cultural promotion.

(3) The plan should be comprehensively calculated, and the extent to which it can be done should be estimated. However, facts are difficult to predict. In the process of implementing the plan, unexpected resistance may be encountered. Therefore, two kinds of limits should be set for the plan, one is the highest limit, and one is the lowest limit.

(4) After the plan is implemented, there should be a report of the results to prove that the plan is not empty talk on paper. (End)

Establishment of the Chinese Chemical Society 158

▲Election of Chen Yuguang and Eight Others as Directors

The convened chemistry discussion meeting was completed on the morning of the 5th. Taking this opportunity, 50 members attending the meeting initiated the organization of the Chinese Chemical Society. The main purpose of the initiative is that the study of chemistry in China has lacked a nationwide organization. For the sake of chemical research for the Chinese nation and for the sake of national defense chemistry, a nationwide organization is imperative. Therefore, the founding meeting was held in the morning at the Overseas Chinese Reception Center. Chen Yuguang and eight others (professors from universities in Beijing, Shanghai, and Beiping were nominated for ease of meeting) were elected as directors. Huang Xinyan and Ge Zhonghe were elected as alternate directors (the first is in Hong Kong and the second is in Henan, so they could not attend the meeting when it was convened, so they were elected as alternate directors). In the afternoon, a board meeting was held to discuss the direction of the society's work and to establish various committees for separate research and to edit publications, it is said.

Sports

Third Rotary Cup, China's Initial Battle Extremely Advantageous 159

China Wins Two Singles Against Portugal

America Wins One Singles Against England

China vs. Portugal, England vs. America, Double Matches This Afternoon

The third Rotary Cup International Tennis Tournament kicked off yesterday. Players from the four participating countries, China, the United States, England, and Portugal, took to the court and worked hard to fulfill their respective missions. Unexpectedly, four to five hundred people gathered on the Chinese tennis court, some said it was a miniature of the World Davis Cup. Within three hours, the result of the four countries' players competing was that China won two singles matches against Portugal, and the United States won a singles match against England. There was also a singles match between England and the United States that was not played due to a misunderstanding on the time of both sides, and will be decided by the committee tomorrow. Starting at 3:00 PM today, England vs. America and China vs. Portugal will hold doubles matches.

China's two singles were represented by Lin Baohua and Zheng Zhaojia, while Portugal was represented by Xiao Tofoska and Navarro. Portugal's fighting strength is far inferior to before, and both singles matches were lost in straight sets.

(1) Lin Baohua Calmly Defeats Opponent 160

Lin Baohua (China) 6-2 6-2 6-3 Xiao Tofoska (Portugal)

Lin Baohua can still be called one of the top figures in Shanghai tennis. That Xiao Tofoska is only a second- or third-rate player. It is a well-known fact that he is controlled by Lin and runs under his command. In the first set, Xiao Tofoska inexplicably captured the second and fifth games, and the remaining lost games were lost without knowing what happened. The situation in the second set was also vaguely similar. In short, the power of life and death was in Lin's hands. In the third set, Xiao Tofoska struggled and fought, using all his strength, hoping to recover something. For a while, he tied the score at 3-3, which was the moment of his momentary triumph that day. His fast serve is the best of his various techniques. In addition, he was extremely impatient, so every move made the viewers couldn't help but smile. Lin showed a calm attitude towards this opponent, and his lifelong skills were hidden and not revealed, perhaps because he couldn't bear to use them. As a result, Lin won with a score of 6-2, 6-2, 6-3.

(2) Zheng Zhaojia Forcefully Defeats Veteran 161

Zheng Zhaojia (China) 6-3 8-6 6-1 Canavano (Portugal)

Zheng Zhaojia, who is regarded as the second Lin Baohua and shows unlimited potential, played against the veteran Canavano of Portugal yesterday in the name of the Chinese team. After three rounds of drumming, applause rose from all sides. The old general abandoned his armor and fled, and the young hero returned in triumph. Zheng has many great records in his own battle history, defeating Takei, defeating Huite, and once defeating De Fu at Lushan. Now he has also heard of defeating Canavano. Zheng Zhaojia's past is like this, he can be the leader of the new generation of masters without shame. As for the rest of the future, I hope he will become one of the famous masters in the Far East as soon as possible. I think Zheng has been thinking and planning about this early on. Canavano lost, but those who watched the game from the sidelines, except for seeing him slightly weak in the third set, still maintained his general demeanor. As a result, Zheng won in straight sets with a score of 6-3, 8-6, 6-1.

▲Catching up later

In the first set, Canavano served first and was cautious. He won the first game. Zheng had the potential to win in the second game, but still failed, because he was impatient. Zheng won the third game without losing a ball. Zheng made many unforced errors in the fourth game and eventually failed, making it 1-3, taking the upper hand. The audience felt cold, but unexpectedly, this aroused the young man's heroic spirit, and he caught up later. He turned danger into safety in the fifth game and won it. The victory in the sixth game depended on the strength of his serve. Zheng had a superhuman performance in the seventh, eighth, and ninth games. He was able to cope with the attacks and was good at attacking. As a result, he won them one by one, resulting in a 6-3 victory.

▲Struggling hard

In the second set, Zheng served first. Canavano was distracted and lost four consecutive points. The first game also belonged to Zheng. Zheng lost his balance in the second game and made many unforced errors. This game went to Canavano (1-1). Each won one game in the third and fourth games, splitting the difference. The fifth and sixth games were the most exciting. Both sides were evenly matched and it was difficult to tell who was better. As a result, Canavano won the fifth game, and Zheng won the sixth game. After the score was tied at 3-3, Canavano swept back and forth, and every serve was extremely fast and difficult to resist. As a result, Zheng was controlled by him and lost the seventh and eighth games, creating an unfavorable situation of 3-5. The ninth game was a matter of life and death. Canavano had a great momentum to take it all down. Soon he took a 3-1 lead. At that time, Zheng calmly responded to the battle, focusing all his attention on attack and defense, escaping from death, turning defeat into victory, and making it 4-5. Zheng won the tenth game in a row, making it 5-5. Waves suddenly rose from the flat ground. Canavano won the eleventh game. From the twelfth game to the fourteenth game, Zheng devoted all his energy to the match, and Canavano didn't know what to do and allowed himself to be slaughtered. As a result, Zheng won again with a score of 8-6.

▲Completing it in one breath

The third set was a one-sided situation. Canavano seemed to have lost his combat ability. He repeatedly changed his strategy, but it was ineffective. After Zheng won two games, Canavano took one game. After this, it was Zheng's world again. Canavano was at his command. As a result, Zheng won again with a score of 6-1.

(3) Squire Defeats Stock 162

Squire (USA) 6-4 7-5 6-3 Stock (England)

In the battle between American player Squire and British player Stock, although the former won in straight sets, every game and set was very close, and even just moving a hand up and down took a lot of effort. The reason why the winner won was that the difference in skills was very small. After 1-1, 2-2, 3-3, and 4-4 in the first set, Squire managed to launch a series of attacks and won with a score of 6-4. Stock was very successful in the second set, and the game turned into an extremely advantageous position of 5-2. What is easily gained is also easily lost. Between the moments, Squire won five consecutive games and turned the game to a 7-5 victory. At the beginning of the third set, Squire took advantage of the victory and made it 5-1 in one fell swoop. Stock tried hard to resist, and although there was a slight improvement, he eventually failed with a score of 3-6.

Yu Binqi and Others Initiate Sino-Western Men's and Women's Swimming Competition 166

▲To Be Held at Mingyuan

Advocates of swimming, Yu Binqi, Hong Zunsan, Wang Jianxin, and others, realizing the immaturity of the Chinese people's swimming skills and the lack of instructors, believe that it is necessary to compete with Chinese and Westerners as a mirror. They visited Mr. Jimi, the manager of Mingyuan, last night and decided on the following methods: gathering gentlemen and ladies from various countries to hold a major swimming competition, which is scheduled to be held at 8:00 PM on the 12th. The events are: (1) 50-meter freestyle, (2) 100-meter backstroke, (3) 25-meter freestyle (women), (4) 100-meter freestyle, (5) 25-meter backstroke (women), (6) 200-meter breaststroke, (7) 25-meter breaststroke (women), (8) 400-meter freestyle, (9) Water floating distance, (10) Fancy diving. The prizes are: gold medals for the first place in each event, silver medals for the second place, and bronze medals for the third place, which are made by Ximen Standard Sports Company. A large silver shield will be awarded as the individual championship, all of which will be borne by Mingyuan. The scoring method is based on the 5-3-2-1 system. The registration place is Jimi's Western Restaurant next to the Sichuan Road Navy Youth Association. Each person is limited to register for three events. After registration, a Mingyuan monthly season ticket will be issued - from the date of registration to the 12th, you can enter the park for free practice at any time, and admission tickets are also free of charge. It is hoped that Shanghai's swimming masters will register as soon as possible, so that they can practice purely, win the championship.

Track and Field Approaching Completion; Interest Shifts to Swimming 173

▲ American Team Certain to Win Track and Field Relay

Electrified News Agency, Los Angeles, 5th. The 6th will be the eighth day of the Games. Track and field events, except for a couple of events like the marathon, will soon be completed. Afterward, the focus of interest will shift to swimming. The swimming and water polo competitions will begin on the 6th, and the crowds that have been gathering at the grandstands will move to the swimming pool.

Swimming events include the 100-meter freestyle preliminary rounds and semifinals, the women's 100-meter freestyle and the women's 200-meter breaststroke preliminary rounds. Water polo competitions will be held twice, in the morning and afternoon.

In the 100-meter freestyle, Waszmola (USA) took first place at the 1928 Amsterdam Games, followed by Barani (Hungary) in second place and Takaishi Katsuo (Japan) in third. However, Waszmola has retired from the athletic association and will not be participating this time. His successors include the famous Galili brothers and other emerging athletes, who will undoubtedly compete fiercely with Japan for the championship. Competition is expected to be intense. Hungary and France also have outstanding talents. The sprint events are expected to be highly competitive.

In the women's 100-meter freestyle at the previous Games, Ausiboz (USA) came in first, Raji (USA) second, and Cuba (England) third. This year, Miss Madison is likely to take first place because she recently broke Ausiboz's Olympic record of 1 minute, 11 seconds, shortening it by 6 seconds to 1 minute, 5 seconds, and setting a new world record.

In track and field, in addition to the second half of the decathlon final, there will also be the 400-meter and 1600-meter relay preliminary rounds and the 3000-meter steeplechase final.

Finland is expected to dominate the 3000-meter steeplechase. The United States is certain to win the 400-meter relay. The 1600-meter relay will also be dominated by the United States. At the previous Games, the American team in the 1600-meter relay, consisting of Bayard, Arda, Spencer, and Barb, set a record of 3 minutes, 14.2 seconds. This year's American team, consisting of Eastman, William Carr, and Gorton, is expected to further shorten the record and set a new one.

Other events include sailing races held at the Los Angeles pier. Athletes who participated in swimming today will also participate in the modern pentathlon after landing. All of these are very interesting events. However, the modern pentathlon ends today.

Municipal Bureau of Education Regularly Distributes July Funds 175

▲ Distributed in Four Days Starting from the 8th of This Month

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education issued a notice yesterday regarding the regular distribution of July funds to its affiliated institutions, stating that the Bureau will distribute the July funds and preliminary school subsidies to its affiliated municipal institutions over four days, from August 8th to 11th, from 8:00 AM to 12:00 PM and 1:00 PM to 3:30 PM daily. Institutions receiving funds during this period should pay attention to the following points: (1) If the revenue reports and verification forms for the 20th academic year's school construction funds have not been submitted, they should be collected and submitted to the Bureau for review and forwarded to the Finance Bureau. (2) If there are still transfer procedures for school construction funds, institutions should bring the payment receipts and verification forms. (3) Institutions should first prepare and submit the expenditure calculation reports for the recurring expenses from February to June of the 20th academic year before receiving the funds. (4) Institutions should also prepare and report the results of the temporary expenses for the 20th academic year for review. (5) Schools should first fill out and submit the monthly fund survey form for the current semester issued by the Bureau before receiving the funds. The fund distribution schedule is as follows: (8th) Yangsi, Yinhang, Pusong, Fahua, Zhabei; (9th) Hunan, Tangqiao, Gaohang, Pengpu, Caojing; (10th) Luxing, Yangjing, Zhenru, Yinxiang, Jiangwan, Wusong; (11th) Gaoqiao, social education institutions, private school subsidies, custodian fees.

Gold Bar Prices Suddenly Show Strength 177

▲ Breaking Through the 740 Tael Barrier

Yesterday, gold bar prices showed unusual strength, breaking through the 740 tael barrier once again. Progressing steadily with small retreats after large gains, prices rose nearly six taels in half a day. Market sentiment among traders was strong, with demand exceeding supply. The market opened steadily. Although silver prices rose, exchange rates continued to plummet, stimulating the depreciation of the US dollar. The forward rate was initially firm but then softened, showing a long position in appearance but easing in reality. In the end, Hengxing and other shorts aggressively covered their positions, and some speculated that a certain bank was opening positions in physical gold. As a result, prices soared, showing a sharp upward trend. The gray market even reached above 43 taels. Because the market will be closed on Saturday, and considering that the market situation has been fluctuating this week without significant changes, from the highest price of 46.2 taels at the beginning of the week, followed by a weakening of foreign exchange rates that broke through 40 taels, to the final price of 35.6 taels on Friday due to the continued decline in exchange rates and a sudden reversal upward, the total difference for the week was 11.6 taels, with a net drop of 4 taels. The detailed market conditions yesterday are recorded below.

▲ Increase of 5.8 Taels

The September contract opened at 737.2 taels, slightly higher by 7 qian. Although the major bars and the American bank rose by a quarter, private telegrams rose slightly by one-sixteenth. Furthermore, the exchange rate plummeted by three fen, reversing market sentiment. The market opened high. Hengxing, Yuanshunli, Yifeng, Yongwanxing, and others showed strong selling intentions, immediately dropping the price by one tael to 6.7 qian. In an instant, Yuanmao, Yonghengchang, Yongheng, Yuhong, Kangyong, Dayong, and Runyong were buying aggressively. Hengxing and Yuanfu were also buying strongly, pushing the price up by 2 taels. At 9:15, the price was 39 taels. The China Merchants Bank started absorbing the October gold from the Bank of England at 9 pence, and the Meifeng, Citibank, and Hua Bi absorbed August US dollars at 125. At this time, Yifeng, Yongheng, Yude, Cheng Yuhe, and others were selling off. HSBC sold August US dollars to Zhengjin at 0625, causing the price to fall back slightly by 1.23 qian to 7.7 qian. Hengxing, Tong Taichang, Yongfeng, and others entered the market to buy, pulling up the price by 1.1 qian to 8.8 qian. News came that the Bank of England had extended the forward rate by one level, bringing the price to 38 taels. However, the US dollar only increased by 125, which was a minor exchange rate adjustment. The domestic market was stable. Hengxing, Yongfeng, Zhifeng, Yong Yifeng, Yongheng Xingyuan, Fuyuanyuan, Taifu, and Taiheng competed to buy, while the Huarbi absorbed the October US dollar at 3125 and the Macalli absorbed the November US dollar at 4375, pushing the market price above 40 taels. At 10:00, the price was 40.5 taels. Hengxing and Yuanfu came out to sell, dropping the price back to 39.2 taels. Afterward, buying interest intensified. Hengxing, Zhaofeng, Changtong Taichang, Hengyu, and Taibang, Yuanmao Yong, and others all entered the market. Furthermore, HSBC absorbed the August Bank of England gold at 8125, and the American Commercial Bank absorbed 30 yuan of US dollars, causing the price to rebound by 2 taels. From 10:15 to 11:00, the price fluctuated slightly by a few qian. At 11:15, the price rose to 41.2 taels. At this time, the Central Bank absorbed 105 physical bars, further boosting confidence. Hengxing Yong Zhifeng Yonglai exited, surpassing 2 taels to 40.03 taels. Afterwards, shorts aggressively covered their positions, with Tong Taichang Da Decheng Boxin Yuan Run Chang Yu Zhou Feng Heng and others buying actively. In half an hour, the price soared by 2 taels to 42.4 taels. The market closed at 42.3 taels, a rebound of 5.8 taels compared to the previous evening. After the close, small shorts continued to enter, and physical deliveries were also delayed, pushing the price up to 43.45 taels. The closing price was essentially even. Because of the Saturday closing, the price of the major bars still increased by 8.5 taels.

▲ Official Price Reduced by 8 Taels

The official price was revised to 807 taels because the US dollar was listed at a premium of 125, totaling 70 to 65 taels, 8 taels less than the previous day. The registered price was 42 taels, and the supplemental tax was 40 taels.

▲ Active Trading in the Market

Trading on the trading floor was very active, with buyers dominating. Statistics show that Hengxing, Hengchang Yong, Yuankangxiang, Tong Dachang, Tong Fenghang, Qianchangxiang, Futaiheng, Yuantai, Yongfeng, Runchangyu, Hongkangyong, Zhaofengchang, and Dakang were all actively buying. Zhifeng Yong, Da Decheng, Hengyu, Wanxing, Shunli, Yuanxing Yong, and Yuhe were all actively trading in and out. Hengxing Yuan traded a total of several thousand bars, with more buying than selling. Yuanmao Yong exited and then re-entered. Yifeng Yong, Taifengcheng, and small traders were all selling. Demand and supply were complex among other firms. Physical deliveries were sold when prices rose and bought when prices fell. Forward exchange contracts were all being bought. The total value of gold bar contracts was approximately 22,000. Hengxing was still short 4,000 to 5,000 bars. Yuanxing Yong was long 4,000 to 5,000, but both had decreased compared to before. No other firms had significant positions.

Cotton Market Buyers' Attitude Hardens 184

The cotton market is trending firm, as American cotton is stable, gold prices have risen again, and sentiment is increasingly positive. Moreover, the bottom inventory of local cotton is extremely scarce, and buyers are eager. Although some major players are selling, the market is not significantly affected. Furthermore, the recent weather has been too dry, hindering the growth of new cotton.

Last Week's American Cotton Banks Raise Funds to Increase Cotton and Wheat Prices 187

▲Dry and Hot Weather in the South

New York, August 5th telegram reports the market conditions for the week: The improvement in commercial sentiment, coupled with the active market prices of miscellaneous grains and securities, has kept the raw cotton market stable throughout the week. The market was particularly firm at the end of the week, coinciding with reports that bankers were planning to raise US$30 million in funds to increase the prices of wheat and cotton. At the beginning of the week, raw cotton continued to be sold. In the past three weeks, cooperatives have sold a total of about 200,000 bales, but this amount has been absorbed by short covering and purchases by the industry. Long positions closing and evening up have curbed the upward trend of cotton prices. The reason for the closing and evening up of positions is that the government's cotton production report will be released on Monday. Due to dry and hot weather in Texas, many places have reported cotton bolls falling off and opening prematurely. At the same time, according to some reports from the eastern cotton belt, the reduced use of fertilizers, unfavorable weather, and damage from boll weevils have reduced the potential for production by 40% compared to the same period last year. However, some cotton merchants are questioning whether the degradation of cotton production is more severe than usual. According to private estimates, the average condition of cotton crops at the end of July was 68%, compared to 74% last month, estimating the number of bales to be around 12,168,000. ▲Xinzha Yesterday, more than 20 suppliers arrived from various routes. Trading on this street was sluggish and stagnant. Foreign Rice Stable in the Morning, Rising in the Afternoon 190

Yesterday, the foreign rice market was initially stable and then rose, with the situation becoming more stable. Sentiment was very good in the morning, but demand was not strong. Only Yongbang slightly purchased old Xiaojiao rice. Retailers on this street did not see large purchases, and the market turned from firm to soft. In the afternoon, Nanjing, Zhenjiang, and Wuxi merchants rushed to purchase in the market. Although the transaction volume was not high, the market price increased by three to five fen. A total of 5,000 bags of Xiaojiao rice were sold at prices ranging from 9.55 yuan to 9.32 yuan. Old Xiaojiao rice was sold at 9.15 yuan. 300 bags of Saigon No. 1 rice were sold at 10.03 yuan. 100 bags of Annam japonica rice were sold at 11.60 yuan. The market turned firm and stable. If demand becomes stronger again, the market price has the potential to rise. However, with the stock decreasing, the holders' sentiment turned firm, and sentiment was no longer as uncertain as before.

Tianjin Merchants Sell Off 150,000 Bags of Spot Flour 191

▲Standards Generally Stable

After the flour market opened yesterday morning, the market for each month was generally stable. As the quoted price of foreign wheat improved by about three jiao, the sentiment outside the industry tended to be stable. However, factories such as Fuxin and Gaofeng, either due to the accumulation of spot goods or the hedging of foreign wheat, successively sold off their inventories. Therefore, although inland merchants unanimously looked bullish due to the drought, they failed to raise prices. As for Tianjin merchants, it was heard that they sold off 150,000 bags of spot flour, including 100,000 bags of "Warship" brand and 50,000 bags of "Artillery Car" brand. Judging from this, spot sales are still active, and the flour market may be able to hold its ground. As a result, this month improved by 2.5 li compared to the previous day, September improved by 5 li, October improved by 2.5 li, November improved by 5 li, and December improved by 7.5 li.

Term Wheat Initially Popular, Then Weak 192

▲Continued Order of Foreign Wheat Confirmed

Yesterday, after the term wheat market opened in the morning, the market for each month showed a trend of initial stability followed by weakness. Initially, the sentiment was good because the quoted price of foreign wheat rose by three jiao. However, because most large holders sold off positions, and Dingtai also sold off a significant amount, and it was heard that another shipment of foreign wheat was ordered at a price that remained a secret, selling pressure was very strong. Near-term and long-term contracts both weakened and fell sharply. Although the millers' wheat inventory was not very abundant, the accumulated flour inventory was generally between 2 million bags, so the demand for wheat will be temporarily shelved. As a result, this month fell by four fen compared to the previous day, September and October fell by six fen, and November and December fell by five fen. The spot wheat market was still stable and popular. Suqian wheat, because of its high quality, opened at a high spot price for the first time, with 800 bags opening at 3.55 yuan. It was also reported that Huafeng and Shenda factories withdrew 30 truckloads of spot wheat from the exchange yesterday at a price of 3.49 yuan. A continued order of foreign wheat was confirmed at a price of 4.10 yuan, which was purchased by inland factories.

Dried and Preserved Goods Cantonese Dried Longan Prices Upside Down 193

The price of Jinshan dried longan has fallen again in the past two days. For example, the price of superior grade flat dried longan has fallen to 25 to 26 yuan, the price of superior grade yuan dried longan is around 25 yuan, and the price of secondary grade ranges from 21 to 22 yuan. The initial price of top-grade glutinous rice dried longan once approached 82 yuan, but has now fallen to about 64 yuan. It is reported that the land price also once fell to 105 yuan, but recently it has rebounded because the goods shipped from the production area are better than before and the body is gradually drying out. Therefore, the land price has rebounded to 130 yuan, and the conversion to Shanghai currency requires more than 70 yuan, which has created an upside-down situation. It is also difficult to convert other Jinshan yuan dried longan and flat dried longan completely. It is expected that the arrival of the Shanghai market price drop telegram may ease the situation.

Additional Import Duty on Raw Silk 195

Due to the economic panic in various countries around the world, import duties are being increased to make up for losses. The Ministry of Finance of our country, in view of the strange deficit in customs revenue in recent times and the increasing sales of new-style silk fabrics, and the frequent import of foreign silk (such as Japanese silk), has specifically increased the import duty on raw silk from 30% to 60%, which was announced and implemented on the 4th.

Miscellaneous Talks

Persistence 203

— Zhanlu

Whenever a pressing time comes to make oaths, the typesetting rooms of various newspapers must add some oath characters.

The declarations of important people always say...swear not to retreat. The telegrams of soldiers always say...swear not to surrender. The talks published by responsible figures always say...swear to resist to the death, regardless of any sacrifice. The telegrams sent by various organizations always say...swear to be the backing, and fight the enemy to the death. In addition, farmers have farmers' oaths, workers have workers' oaths, and students have students' oaths. Among many lead characters, only the oath character is active, and only the oath character is busy.

The situation is tense, and oath characters are written in large letters on the wall! The situation is urgent, and oath characters are pasted in large letters on the wall! It is as if the oath character created by the old man Cangjie has become a modern weapon to resist the enemy. In fact, the old man Cangjie was never too clever. The oath character he created implicitly implies that it is not a real price. The oath character has "fold" above and "speech" below. It can be seen that this kind of speech contains a big discount. If the discount is small, it is 90% and 80%. If the discount is large, it is 10% and 20%. The two characters "fold" and "speech" combine to form the oath character. Speech with a discount becomes an oath, and speech without a discount does not become an oath. Thinking from the method of breaking characters, it can be seen that this oath character is unreliable.

Rehe is in danger! The typesetting rooms are adding oath characters again! Anyone who pays attention to current affairs must know the clear attitude of Tang Yulin, the defending general of Rehe. Good! The hot soup has been expressed! He is determined to resist Japan and swears to live and die with the city!

Is the hot soup oath reliable? Don't let it contain another big discount! I say...the oaths of others may be unreliable. The oath of the Tang family must be reliable. Tang said...resist Japan, determined to resist Japan. Tang said...live and die with the city, determined to live and die with the city. This is not my speculation. The ancients have already had foreknowledge. Tang's oath is recorded in the first volume of Mencius, which everyone reads thoroughly.

— Tang swore and said; when will this day perish? I and you shall perish together!

The Demeanor of New China 204

— Genxin

The demeanor of New China is difficult to describe completely. It is appropriate to use the phrase "Good Weather for the Crops, National Peace and Prosperity" on the top of the Great Buddha Hall as a conclusion. Chinese people who respect etiquette and civilization are by no means weak and incompetent, and are ridiculed as the "Sick Man of East Asia." In the past 20 years, the martial spirit has prevailed throughout the country. The number of warriors under the command of generals is about several million, as well as the numerous brave and adventurous bandits, which can be seen in general. Furthermore, for the sake of strengthening strength, special attention is paid to practical exercises (ie, so-called civil war).

Recently, some people have advocated "aiming the guns outward," which is again contrary to the dignity of our country of etiquette. Therefore, the authorities have always held high the champagne glasses and offered them to my dear tributary states.

China is blessed with beautiful mountains and rivers. Therefore, even courageous generals have a light and tranquil nature and an attitude of appreciating art. When they come to Mount Tai, Mount Wutai, Mount Lu, Kuling, Mount Emei, West Lake, Beidaihe, etc., they are either avoiding the summer heat or claiming illness, or chanting Buddha or holding meetings. And a romantic general who has always lived in the cold regions has held dozens of meetings with various pretexts in recent years. It is said that they do not speak at the meetings, but use their mouths for banquets, and after the banquets, they go sightseeing. They are full of energy and everyone is happy. This is a manifestation of the spirit of democracy.

There are also elementary school students singing the party song, middle school students becoming committee members, and university students going out to participate in activities.

Modern people are doing ABCD (ie, the first letters of the French words for love, beauty, song, and dance). It can truly be said that they are "working tirelessly day and night, and following the ideology."

Most literati and writers use artistic skills and vivid writing to create interesting texts that cater to the psychology of young people. In addition, for the sake of providing young people with shortcuts to learning, they create large-scale question-and-answer guides, outlines, and summaries. This is also the supreme glory of the publishing world in New China.

The activity of the party and the large number of participants clearly show the enthusiasm of the people to "jointly overcome national difficulties."

After the conclusion of the boycott movement, blue-eyed high officials may have to send congratulatory telegrams to our people, and first to the modern men and women.

Chinese movie theaters are springing up like mushrooms after rain, introducing the romantic affairs of the highest peaks in the world, and hinting at one of the ways out for Chinese youth.

Newspapers are routinely prepared to publish moving social news and sports news in large columns, as well as more than half of the advertisements that suit people's tastes.

Recently, there are even dazzling, colorful film newspapers appearing, which are one of the bibles for film fans.

Everyone says "national crisis is imminent," but enjoyment is still enjoyed. In a word, it is all "contradiction"!

The Middle School Student's Predicament 205

— Zhang Yunfei

The other day, upon reading an article titled "The Middle School Student's Predicament" in (Freedom Forum), my heart resonated with infinite sympathy. Speaking from my own experience, after ten years of diligent study and dedicated effort, I finally obtained a middle school diploma from a prestigious Shanghai school this summer. However, what will happen after graduation? This significant (?) always lingers in my mind.

Should I pursue further education? But pursuing further education is not easy either. First, it requires financial ease. Universities are institutions for the children of the wealthy. Ordinary poor students can only stop short. After solving the economic problem, there is still the significant issue of finding a university. I have already hesitated considerably in this matter. There are now over forty universities in China, but how many of them can truly satisfy people? Some universities are superficial and impractical, aiming solely to cultivate a large group of gentlemen and ladies. Some universities are controlled by politicians, becoming battlegrounds for political parties. Still other universities are corrupt beyond imagination, with diplomas being given out indiscriminately. I ask, would a thoughtful young person be willing to apply to such a university? Truly, from my observation, I feel that apart from a few universities in Beiping—Yenching and Tsinghua, etc.—there are practically no good schools. However, Beiping is facing a precarious situation, with rumors flying and an imminent crisis, deterring most scholars.

Then, should I look for a job? Humph! What can a middle school student do? The authorities of middle schools never think about middle school students finding jobs. They simply fail to instill knowledge about social service in the minds of middle school students. As a result, they create a large group of high-level idlers who only know how to consume and not produce. I am inevitably one of them, with nothing to do at all.

The above is the pain I feel personally. I hope that educators who run universities and middle schools in the future can undertake reforms to prevent a large group of middle school students from being at a loss about their future.

Random Notes on Amber 206

— Qin Bowen

Having read Mr. Ninety-Three's article "(The Miracle of the Traveling Herbalist)" in this publication, I will offer my knowledge for discussion. Mr. Ninety-Three's article can be divided into three points: 1. The authenticity of amber; 2. The origin of amber; 3. Why amber can cure heart disease.

Now, amber is a mineral with many varieties. Lei Xiao stated that the genuine amber is red as blood. When rubbed against cloth, the genuine kind attracts mustard seeds. Amber imported from Japan is transparent with a deep red color. The Chinese call it blood amber or gold amber. This is the best quality. The slightly lighter color is called silver amber, the second best. Light yellow amber is called wax amber, the next best. The amber with black color is considered inferior. (Mr. Ninety-Three mentioned that most of the amber seen in the country is dark crystal color, which belongs to this kind.) See the Daily Use Medicine Examination.

Regarding the name of amber, Li Shizhen said, "(When a tiger dies, its spirit enters the earth and turns into stone. This object resembles it, so it is called tiger's spirit. The common writing uses jade because it is similar to jade.)" Let us continue with this explanation.

Its origin is due to the resin of coniferous plants, buried in the ground, which turns into stone over a long time. Therefore, it is often found in the third and fourth underground layers, scattered among small stones of sand, clay, and limestone. Amber obtained from the seashore probably comes from the underground layers. It is mostly produced along the coasts of East Asia, and in sand or seawater in countries such as Russia, Germany, Poland, Sweden, and Denmark. The Book of Han, Records of the Western Regions, stated that amber comes from foreign countries. The elders passed down the legend that amber is transformed from pine resin, which is not unfounded. It is indeed a transformed stone tree gum, not a kind of wood resin. Some specifically refer to the resin of pine and maple. However, wood resin turns into stone after being buried for thousands of years, but it does not age as much as the resin of pine and maple.

Amber can cure heart disease, as seen in medical books. It is not a secret exclusively known by traveling herbalists. However, the so-called heart disease is limited to symptoms such as heart pain, restlessness, epilepsy, and other ailments. The reason is that its components are resin, volatile oil, succinic acid, succinoresinol, and sulfur, etc. The contained penetrating and volatile oil-salts have the effect of opening up the brain's nerves. External use is effective for treating local paralysis and chronic joint rheumatism. However, there is no evidence to support the traveling herbalist's use of it for treating palpitations.

Additionally, amber oil is a very effective rat poison. Its effective ingredient is succinic acid. The method is to mix succinic acid with ox bile and buckwheat flour that rats like to eat, and make them into pills. Rats eat it and immediately become covered in bristling hair, feel thirsty and want to die. They drink water if they can get it, but the more they drink, the thirstier they become. Gradually, their movements become sluggish. Within three and a half to twenty-seven hours after eating, they all die. See the Tokyo Veterinary New Report, which is not found in Chinese medical books. (Thank you)

Worth Recommending National Goods Factories (19) 207

— He Gongxing

(3) (10) Foot Flower Textile Factory

Cotton spinning and weaving is one of the major industries in our country. However, few know how to utilize the leftover foot flowers (cotton waste), which are sold to foreigners at a low price to manufacture products such as blankets, absorbent cotton, and toys, and then imported back into the country. The profit made in this one turnaround is enormous. The scale of the leakage is imaginable. In recent years, the Shanghai Minsheng Yarn Factory has taken the lead in utilizing foot flowers and engaging in waste spinning. This was followed by the Tongcheng Textile Company, and then six or seven factories such as Jingwei, Qinfeng, and Shenxin followed suit. In particular, Tongcheng Textile Company has the most complete equipment, with spinning, weaving, bleaching, and dyeing all available. The factory is located in Qishuyan, Changzhou, on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, covering an area of over 160 acres. It borders the canal to the south and the railway to the north. Within the factory, the industrial operations are divided into a cotton production department, a bleaching and dyeing department, a spinning department, and a weaving department. The machines are all purchased from famous German factories, arranged neatly, and fully equipped. The products include 4-count and 6-count coarse yarn, gray military blankets, patterned and plain flannelette, shuttlecocks, socks, scarves, and absorbent cotton gauze. Among them, the flannelette blankets and flannelette are brightly colored and sturdy. The gray military blankets are produced in the hundreds of thousands each year and are of excellent quality. The factory's products have been selling very well in recent years because they are cheaper and of better quality compared to foreign goods. In terms of factory management, they are quite able to cater to the trends of the times and treat their employees very well, with facilities such as a cooperative, a clinic, a small school, a garden, and a bathroom. The factory interior and exterior are unusually spacious, with lush trees, so that even in the height of summer, it does not feel hot. It can accommodate more than a thousand workers. Although there is no labor union organization, the relationship between labor and management is harmonious.

Records of Knocking on the Bell at Ancient Temples (67) 208

— Butingcaozhaitian

74

I asked: (What conditions are necessary for a work-study group to succeed?) Mr. Zhu said: (First, there must be the determination to start it; second, there must be the technical skills to work; third, there must be available raw materials; fourth, there must be labor; and fifth, there must be capital.)

I asked: (If we start a work-study group in a traditional school, the determination to start lies in the change of attitude; the technical skills to work can be learned with an open mind; the available raw materials are naturally locally sourced; labor is readily available, and the willingness to use it is also a matter of a change of mind; but the capital, in this time of national poverty, how can it be obtained?)

Mr. Zhu said: (It is readily available! As long as we change our minds, the great capital is right in front of our eyes and we do not need to ask others. Go to the Ministry of Education and find the recently published Education Statistics Overview, and we can calculate how much capital we can use.)

75

We obtained some astonishing facts from the statistics of the Ministry of Education and other sources. From August of the 7th year of the Republic of China to July of the 18th year, there were 86 registered public and private universities and specialized schools nationwide, with 6,985 faculty and staff members, 53,410 students, and an expenditure of 36.79 million yuan. There were 1,339 public and private secondary schools nationwide, including those not registered, with 30,348 faculty and staff members, 234,811 students, and an expenditure of 24.6 million yuan. The personal expenses of university students were about 300 yuan per person per year, totaling 16.02 million yuan. The personal expenses of middle school students were about 150 yuan per person per year, totaling 35.22 million yuan. Adding personal expenses to school expenses, the 86 universities and specialized schools consume 52.82 million yuan of national strength per year, and the 1,339 secondary schools consume 59.82 million yuan of national strength per year. The total annual consumption of schools above the middle school level is 112.64 million yuan. This consumption is spent every year, and continuing to consume it for ten years means that 1,126.4 million yuan will vanish into thin air. We are simply teaching people to sit idle and deplete their resources by running some schools that do not engage in production. If everyone changes their minds and schools become work-study groups, this annual consumption of 112.64 million yuan will immediately turn into productive capital, and 37,000 teachers and 287,000 students will transform from high-level idlers into productive workers. The 86 universities, each with 600,000 yuan of capital, would become a medium-sized factory. The 1,339 secondary schools, each with 46,000 yuan of capital, would become a small factory. Since capital is used for production, it will roll up year after year. After ten years, each medium-sized factory would have 6 million yuan of capital and become a large factory, and each small factory would have 460,000 yuan of capital and become a medium-sized factory. In this way, we can turn a poor China into a rich China. If we do not change our minds, we will lose both people and money, and we will all lament, "Alas? Chinese nation?" This idea must be changed quickly!

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Essay

The Reasons for the Occurrence of Emotion and the True Meaning of Emotion 209

— Lin Xia

This publication has already published many excellent articles on issues such as fidelity, remarriage, marriage, suicide, and sexual desire. I feel that these issues contain a fundamental major issue, which is the word (emotion).

The ancients discussed emotion by focusing on the superficial meaning and nature, praising things like emotional obsession, emotional seed, true emotion, false emotion, passion, cold emotion, emotion of utmost sincerity, pure emotion, etc. There is truly no end to the list. However, the reasons for the occurrence of emotion and the true meaning of emotion have not been mentioned even once.

Humans are the animals most rich in emotion, so to study the word "emotion," we cannot find its true meaning by focusing solely on human activities. It is best to use a biological perspective to examine the phenomena of the animal kingdom, and then we will understand.

The occurrence of emotion in the animal kingdom is gradually evolving. The lowest animals cannot be said to have any emotion. Their bodies are simple, they live independently, reproduce by fission, have no distinction between male and female, and slightly higher animals only temporarily join (not mate) for a moment during the breeding season and then separate, still living and dying independently. It is difficult to speculate whether there is any emotion between the two bodies.

In higher animals, such as insects, fish, frogs, birds, and beasts, most also mate during the breeding season. At this time, between the two bodies, in order to seek the propagation of the species, various joyful (feelings) naturally appear. Fierce creatures such as tigers, leopards, and venomous creatures such as snakes and scorpions also become gentle at this moment. However, after this once, they scatter in different directions, and the root of emotion remains weak. Only spiders are heartless and extremely cruel. After mating, the male often faces the misfortune of being killed and eaten by the female, which can be considered a unique exception in the animal kingdom.

A few higher birds, such as sparrows and swallows, and a few beasts, such as apes and monkeys, after mating, the male and female still live together and raise their young together. Thus, the emotion of mutual affection and love becomes even stronger, and the duration of love also becomes longer. However, when the chicks grow wings, they fly away on their own. When the calves have feet, they run away without saying goodbye. An old couple, because the responsibility of reproduction has come to an end, also sings a farewell song and declares a divorce on their own without a judge's ruling. In the coming year, they each seek new lovers and live together again, repeating the law of nature's endless cycle. Only the highest gorillas and humans, after mating, live together permanently, with the strongest and longest-lasting emotions. Human society has also created marriage rituals to prevent promiscuity and established laws to prevent variations.

Looking at the entire animal kingdom, I can draw a conclusion: (1) (Emotion) gradually occurs with the evolution of animals. The higher the animal, the stronger and longer-lasting the emotion. Why is there (emotion)? Initially, it was to maintain the species and produce offspring. Therefore, the original (emotion) is entirely the (emotion) of male-female union.

(2) Since the occurrence of (emotion) is built on male-female union, it can be seen that the effect of (emotion) is to make the male and female happily unite, willingly and gladly, to sacrifice energy for the species and raise offspring. This is the true meaning of (emotion).

When animals evolved to the point where males and females live together permanently, then love and filial piety (emotion) arise between parents and children, and brotherly and sisterly (emotion) arise between siblings. Furthermore, harmony, respect, and love (emotion) arise between relatives and friends. The power of these emotions lies in increasing the interest of life and promoting social peace and progress.

Young men and women, the word (emotion) actually contains the roots of duty. If you only talk about love to seek spiritual comfort and physical protection, it is too selfish. If you feel willing to fulfill the responsibility of propagating the species, you might as well embrace celibacy and do some other work that contributes to society. If you are unwilling to abandon the natural duty of reproduction, as long as you choose a partner who is healthy in body and mind and who shares your feelings, you can get married. In this time of crisis, you should not live extravagantly. Once married, you should each fulfill your duties and naturally have a good life. You must not imitate the lower animals and casually break off the relationship. If you commit suicide because of unrequited love, it shows your lack of awareness and misunderstanding of the whole of life. If a couple unfortunately dies young, leaving behind weak children and orphans, a widow's willingness to maintain her fidelity, sacrifice her personal happiness, and complete her unfinished responsibility of raising the children is admirable and worthy of respect. It is wrong to forcibly deprive her of her will. If she has no children and it is difficult to make a living, she is unwilling to give up her duty of being able to reproduce and remarries another, which is in accordance with the great law of nature. How can it be considered a loss of fidelity? As for indulging in physical pleasure and engaging in vulgar behavior, one can only be regarded as an animal. How can that be (human) or (emotion)?
