Science

Immunity 211

— Zhong Rui

The meaning of Immunization is to enable the body to adapt to itself when a foreign protein (Note 1) occurs in the body. It means the ability to resist the aggression of Pathogenic Microorganisms. Immunity is divided into two categories: (1) Passive immunity; (2) Active immunity

(1) Passive Immunity This type of immunization method involves administering Antitoxin or Anti Bacterial serum to the patient. This serum, after being injected into the human body, cannot cause the patient to develop any antitoxic effects on their own, but provides the patient with special resistance factors. These resistance factors are mostly taken from other animals, such as horses and cows. A small amount of pathogens is injected into the body of a horse, and the resistance factors for these pathogens exist in the horse's blood. We devise a way to obtain these resistance factors and store them well, preventing them from being destroyed, and then use them when humans or other animals are infected.

Passive immunity is applied during acute infection to assist in the operation of the patient's internal tissue functions, destroy bacteria, and relieve and neutralize the toxins produced by the bacteria. The effective period of passive immunity substances is very short, and they completely lose their immunity within three weeks after being injected into the body.

(2) Active Immunity The production of active immunity substances occurs when the tissues and cells in the human body interact with Infection, and they must produce a special resistance factor to overcome it. Therefore, active immunity substances are all products of the direct struggle between human cells and infection. After these substances are produced, they often exist in human blood vessels and lymph, and when pathogens invade the body, they eliminate them, preventing the human body from being affected in any way.

Two Methods for Inducing Active Immunity 212

1. Artificial Inoculation This method is applied to healthy people by inoculating the human body with pathogens that have been carefully processed to be less harmful, so as to make a gentle invasion of the human body and avoid the heavy blow of an epidemic infectious disease. For example, the (human pox) used before the invention of cowpox is one example.

2. Vaccination This method involves injecting an antigen to stimulate body tissues to produce resistance factors.

The antigen used for vaccination can be a diluted or limited living germ, such as the smallpox vaccine. Dead bacteria and their toxins can also be used, such as scarlet fever antitoxin serum.

As for epidemic patients who have recovered, they generally no longer develop the disease afterwards because the patient's body, after the natural struggle with the bacteria, has stored a large amount of resistance factors.

(Note 1) Foreign protein is different from the protein originally in the human body. It is toxic to the human body and is mostly an organism that invades from the outside.

Discussion on Social Reform - The Prerequisite for Revitalizing National Goods 213

— He Gongxing

▲Advocate Joint Operations

The failure of national goods factories in the past, although caused by various reasons, was mostly due to jealousy among competitors, ultimately leading to mutual destruction, accounting for seventy or eighty percent.

If an industry is profitable, one person creates it, and a hundred people follow suit. Given the vastness of China's territory, it would not be a problem if a hundred people produced in a hundred different places. Even if that is not the case, with you in the west and me in the east, and a hundred different sales locations, it would not be impossible. However, they prefer to gather in one corner and compete in one corner, leading to mutual jealousy! Competitive selling! Price reductions! Changing materials! Skimping on labor! Poor quality products, no one cares, until mutual destruction occurs. Foreigners often mock the Chinese people for being accustomed to internecine strife, and this seems to confirm it.

Our country is a country with backward production. In recent years, the production volume of industrial products in the country is two-fifths of the consumption volume. However, the material progress of society is advancing rapidly. The urgent need of the people for industrial products can be imagined. Various countries even regard our country as a dumping ground for goods. If we use national goods for the adoption of the people, if they are cheap and of good quality, we only need to worry about demand exceeding supply, and not worry about supply exceeding demand. In such a large China, there are many sales channels. Why compete in one corner and insist on mutual destruction?

When the snipe and the clam fight, the fisherman benefits. Watching millions and billions of dollars go across the Atlantic and Pacific Oceans, alas, people come with goods, and we go with money. People come with money, and we go with national sovereignty. Who is really doing this, who is causing this? This is the misfortune of our country's industry and commerce in the past, and it is also the greatest misfortune for the future of the Republic of China.

In fact, our country's manufacturing industry today is still in the stage of competitive manufacturing and has not yet reached the stage of competitive selling. They do not focus on making sturdy and durable products, striving for excellence to last for a long time, but want to sell self-righteous and substandard products for a short time. The reasons for this are nothing more than the following two psychological factors:

(1) Shortage of capital, eager to make a profit. (2) Speculative mentality, changing with trends. With these two types of industrialists, the fate of Chinese manufacturing can be known. Therefore, to maintain our country's current factories, we must advocate joint operations. To resist foreign goods and revitalize national goods, we must first advocate joint operations. There are two prerequisites for joint operations:

(A) Restricting production volume.

(B) Estimating standard prices.

First, statistically determine the annual sales volume of goods in the industry. Allocate the total sales volume to the factories in the same industry for separate manufacturing. Then, stipulate the annual increase in production volume to prepare for the need for annual sales growth. Excessive surplus or insufficiency violates the principle and should be punished. However, the method of allocating production volume is extremely difficult. A slight lack of fairness will cause complaints to arise. Let me tentatively suggest the following methods:

(1) Determine the production volume based on the size of the capital.

(2) Use the average sales volume of each factory in the recent three years as the standard for the factory's production volume in the future.

Factories have different talents, and social needs are also different. If we insist on using capital as the production standard, it will be difficult to be fair. Moreover, there are historical processes and profit and loss relationships, and there are other issues related to whether the capital can maintain the initial amount. These are all sufficient to make the first method difficult. As for using the average sales volume for one or two years as the standard for future production volume, this is based on facts and is more fair. In addition, estimating the standard prices of goods should first involve inviting industry leaders and experts in the industry to collect various goods from the industry, publicly exhibit them, estimate prices, determine the size of the prices according to the quality of the goods, and determine whether the prices should be increased or decreased in the future. In addition to considering raw material wages and other circumstances, we should also consider the volume of sales to determine whether the prices of certain goods should be increased or decreased, which is also very fair. There are five benefits of joint operations:

(1) It is possible to implement an overall plan. (2) It is possible to concentrate talents and promote sales separately. (3) It is possible to focus on manufacturing. (4) It is possible to deal with customers as a whole. (5) It is possible to avoid meaningless competition, resulting in mutual damage.

In short, it can be said that it is difficult to support oneself alone, and many hands make light work. This is not just the case for joint operations. After the operation is combined, the first thing to do is to engage in division of labor manufacturing. If an industry has more than ten colors of goods, it is not necessary for one factory to manufacture all of them. The factory that is usually good at manufacturing a certain color should be responsible for specializing in that product. The industry is skilled in one, one is specialized, specialized is familiar, familiar is fast, fast is more, and the output is more, the cost will be reduced accordingly. However, in addition to being responsible for manufacturing a certain color of goods that they are good at, they must also be responsible for manufacturing one or two additional colors in order to adjust their sales. The products of each factory are different, but social needs are sometimes the same. Therefore, there are times when product A sells well and product B is sluggish. Product A is bound to make a profit and product B will lose money. Starting with profit and ending with harm greatly violates the original purpose of the union. Now, if they also manufacture other types of goods, it is unlikely that several types of goods will sell well at the same time, or be sluggish at the same time. In short, after joint operations, factories in the same industry will share blessings and difficulties, coexist and prosper, advance and retreat together, so as not to waste this unity. Furthermore, it is possible to cooperate in raw materials and consumption, which are all within the possible scope, but they are not related to the main topic, so they should be discussed separately.

The benefits of joint operations have been mentioned above, but there are also disadvantages. Factories have been competing for a long time, and once they reconcile and turn hostility into friendship, it is like returning soldiers after a war, with the sole aim of seeking peace, thinking that there are no strong enemies outside and that they can leisurely enjoy the remaining years. The quality of the products remains the same, with no improvement at all. At the same time, they regard their industry as hereditary, monopolizing one side, and because of the lack of competition in the industry, they are slow and impolite to customers, thinking that if they are needed, who else is there but me. However, these are all personal educational relationships and cannot be said to be the harm of joint operations. Although these are the words of the author's excessive worry, they are also things that may happen. I sincerely hope that these words are not true.

This is the instruction. ▲Huang Shengfu's petition to stop the auction and order payment in cash is noted. Wait for the summons for investigation and decision. This is the instruction. ▲Zhang Jinsong's petition to order Zhang Yusheng to vacate the house and pay rent. ▲Shui Yiren's petition to claim the deposit is noted. Prepare for investigation and decision. This is the instruction. ▲Yu Yongzhou's petition to strictly enforce is noted. The case is ordered to be strictly pursued within a limited time. You have been informed. This is the instruction. ▲Wang Laiqing's petition to claim the case is noted. The case should be cancelled. This is the instruction. ▲Duan Gu'an's petition to cancel the case is noted. The case should be cancelled. This is the instruction. ▲Liu Longbao's petition for execution is noted. Wait for the case to be summoned for execution. This is the instruction. ▲Ye Yongsheng's petition to continue execution is noted. The debtor has already paid the remaining debt in full. Bring the mediation record to the court at 9 a.m. on the 12th of this month to claim the case completion. This is the instruction. ▲Ye Pengyuan's petition to seize is noted. The first and second defendants in this case, Yuan Gongxin, have successively paid 80 yuan, which will be issued at 10 a.m. on the 9th of this month. The request to pay the remaining debt within a limited time is temporarily postponed. This is the instruction. ▲Hua Yude's petition to execute the remaining debt is noted. Wait for continued execution. This is the instruction. ▲Zhu Zhushi's petition for execution is noted. Wait for the case to be summoned for execution. This is the instruction. ▲Yao Ajiang's petition to appoint is noted. The appointment is approved. This is the instruction. ▲Jiang Zi's petition to seize is noted. The amount owed in this case is not much. Wait for the summons to summon and recover it. The request is temporarily postponed. This is the instruction. (Above are from August 6th)
